<span data-ttu-id="997d0-765">如先前所述，您可以將資料從 Access 資料庫匯出為不同的檔案格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-765">As previously explained, you can export data from an Access database to different file formats.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-766">您選擇要匯出的檔案格式可能會取決於來自資料主體的特定 DSR 匯出要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-766">The export file format that you choose might be determined by the specific DSR export request from a data subject.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-767">請參閱[匯入及匯出](https://support.microsoft.com/office/import-and-export-c060505b-d8ac-4499-8879-733e56c6106f)主題清單，其中說明如何以不同的檔案格式匯出 Access 資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-767">See [Import and export](https://support.microsoft.com/office/import-and-export-c060505b-d8ac-4499-8879-733e56c6106f) for a list of topics that describe how to export Access data in different file formats.</span></span>

##### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-768">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-768">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p237">您可以刪除整筆記錄，或只是從 Access 資料庫中刪除一個欄位。從 Access 資料庫中刪除一筆記錄的最快方法，就是以 [資料工作表] 檢視開啟資料表，選取您想要刪除的記錄 (列) 或只選取欄位中的資料，然後按 [刪除]。您也可以使用您為了尋找資料所建立的選取查詢，然後將它轉換為刪除查詢。請參閱：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p237">You can delete an entire record or just a field from an Access database. The quickest way to delete a record from an Access database is to open the table in Datasheet view, select the record (row) or just the data in a field that you want to delete, and then press Delete. You can also use a select query that you created to find data and then convert it to a delete query. See:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-773">從資料庫中刪除一或多筆記錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-773">Delete one or more records from a database</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/ways-to-add-edit-and-delete-records-5e90a80c-106d-4c55-996e-07d7200980ce)
- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-774">建立並執行刪除查詢</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-774">Create and run a delete query</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/create-and-run-a-delete-query-6da65fe1-0fc7-4a64-8ef0-c052cd4c3ec5)

### <a name="business-apps-for-office-365"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-775">適用於 Office 365 的商務應用程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-775">Business Apps for Office 365</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-776">本節說明如何在下列各種適用於 Office 365 的商務應用程式中使用應用程式內功能來回應 DSR 要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-776">This section explains how to use the in-app functionality in each of the following Business Apps for Office 365 to respond to DSR requests.</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-777">Bookings</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-777">Bookings</span></span>](#bookings)
- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-778">Listings</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-778">Listings</span></span>](#listings)
- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-779">Connections</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-779">Connections</span></span>](#connections)

#### <a name="bookings"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-780">Bookings</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-780">Bookings</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p238">下列各節說明如何使用 Microsoft Bookings 中的應用程式內功能，來尋找、存取、匯出及刪除個人資料。這同時適用於獨立的 Bookings 應用程式和透過商務中心存取的 Bookings。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p238">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Bookings to find, access, export, and delete personal data. This applies to both the standalone Bookings app and to Bookings when accessed through the Business center.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p239">Microsoft Bookings 允許系統管理員或使用者或其組織內具有 Bookings 授權的員工設定預約頁面，讓客戶可以排程及變更約會、接收確認電子郵件、更新、取消及提醒電子郵件。企業主及其員工也可以透過 Bookings 代表客戶預約事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p239">Microsoft Bookings allows administrators and users or staff, with a Bookings license in their organization, to set up booking pages so customers can schedule and make changes to appointments, receive confirmation emails, updates, cancellation, and reminders email. Business owners and their staff can also book events on behalf of their customers with Bookings.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-785">以下是客戶、系統管理員或員工所建立的資料類型：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-785">The following types of data are created by customers, administrators, or staff:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-786">**客戶、合作夥伴和朋友的連絡資訊** - 這項資料包含名稱、電話號碼、電子郵件地址、地址及附註。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-786">**Contact information of customers, partners, and friends** - This data contains name, phone number, email address, address, and notes.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="997d0-787">任何人都可以使用 Bookings Web、iOS 及 Android 用戶端，手動建立連絡人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-787">Contacts for anyone can be manually created by using the Bookings Web, iOS, and Android clients.</span></span>
    
    - <span data-ttu-id="997d0-788">任何人都可以透過 Bookings iOS 和 Android 用戶端，將連絡人從 C1 的行動裝置匯入 Bookings 中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-788">Contacts for anyone can be imported from a C1's mobile device into Bookings with the Bookings iOS and Android clients.</span></span>
    
    - <span data-ttu-id="997d0-789">在透過任何預約者的預約工作流程建立預約時，也會自動建立連絡人，不論預約是由使用者代表客戶建立，或是由客戶使用擁有者的預約頁面建立。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-789">Contacts are also auto-created at the time of booking creation through the booking workflow for anyone booked, whether the booking is created by a user on a customer's behalf or if it's created by the customer using the owner's booking page.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-790">**預約事件** - 企業主或其指定員工與客戶之間會有一些會議，這些會議是由企業主或客戶透過企業主的公用預約頁面所建立。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-790">**Booking events** - These are meetings between the business owner or their designated staff and a customer, which are created either by the business owner or the customer through the business owner's public booking page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-791">此資料包括名稱、地址、電子郵件地址、電話號碼，以及企業主在預約時向客戶收集的任何其他資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-791">This data includes name, address, email address, phone number, and any other info the business owner collects from the customer at the time of booking.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-792">**電子郵件確認/取消/更新** - 這些是系統所產生和傳送的特定預約事件相關電子郵件訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-792">**Email confirmations/cancellations/updates** - These are email messages generated and sent by the system in association with specific booking events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-793">其中包含排定要提供相關服務之員工的個人資料，以及包含企業主或客戶在預約時所輸入之客戶的個人資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-793">They contain personal data about the staff who is scheduled to deliver the relevant service and they contain personal data about the customer that was entered by either the business owner or the customer at the time of booking.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p242">所有客戶內容都會儲存在 Exchange Online 信箱中，而該信箱會裝載組織的 Bookings。除非企業主和客戶明確要求刪除資料，或者如果他們離開服務，只要他們仍在服務中，就會保留此內容。此內容可以利用產品內 UI、利用 Cmdlet，或是透過刪除相關的預約信箱來刪除。一旦啟動刪除動作，資料就會在企業主設定的期間內刪除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p242">All customer content is stored in the Exchange Online mailbox that hosts the organization's Bookings. This content is retained for as long as the business owner and customer are active in the service, unless they explicitly request that the data be deleted or if they leave the service. This content can be deleted with in-product UI, with a cmdlet, or through deletion of the relevant booking mailbox. Once the deleted action is initiated, the data is deleted within the time period set by the business owner.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-798">如果客戶決定離開服務，其客戶內容會在 90 天後刪除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-798">If a customer decides to leave the service, their customer contents is deleted after 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-799">如需使用者帳戶刪除後何時會刪除信箱內容的詳細資訊，請參閱[移除 Exchange Online 資料](#removing-exchange-online-data)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-799">For more information about when mailbox content is deleted after a user account in deleted, see [Removing Exchange Online data](#removing-exchange-online-data).</span></span>

#### <a name="end-user-identifiable-information"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-800">使用者識別資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-800">End User Identifiable Information</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p244">使用者識別資訊 (EUII) 包含 Bookings 中已排定員工的相關個人和連絡人資訊。當企業主設定 Bookings 及在設定後進行更新時，此資訊就會新增至員工詳細資料頁面。其中包含員工的名稱、縮寫、電子郵件地址和電話號碼。此資料會儲存在裝載 Bookings 的 Exchange Online 信箱中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p244">End user Identifiable Information (EUII) includes personal and contact information about the staff that gets scheduled in Bookings. It's added to the Staff details pages when the business owner sets up Bookings and makes updates after the setup. It contains staff member's name, initials, email address, and phone number. This data is stored in the Exchange Online mailbox that hosts Bookings.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p245">除非已使用應用程式內 UI 明確地刪除企業主或系統管理員，或刪除相關的預約信箱，否則只要員工仍在服務中，都會保留此資料。當系統管理員開始刪除員工的詳細資料時，或者如果員工離職，就會根據企業主或系統管理員所設定的 Exchange Online 信箱內容保留原則，刪除其詳細資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p245">This data is retained for as long as the staff member is active in the service unless it's explicitly deleted the business owner or an admin using the in-app UI or by deleting the relevant booking mailbox. When the admin initiates the deletion of staff's details, or if the staff member leaves the service, their details are deleted in accordance with the Exchange Online mailbox's content retention policies set by the business owner or admin.</span></span>

##### <a name="discoveraccess"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-807">探索/存取</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-807">Discover/Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-808">Bookings 會收集並儲存下列類型的資料：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-808">Bookings gather and store the following types of data:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-809">**企業設定檔資訊：** 使用 Bookings 之企業的相關客戶內容是透過 Bookings 的企業資訊表單來收集，而如果客戶使用 Bookings 搭配商務中心，則此內容就會與商務中心的企業設定檔同步處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-809">**Business profile information:** Customer content about the business using Bookings is collected through the Bookings' Business information form and is synchronized with the Business Center Business Profile if a customer is using Bookings along with the Business center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-810">與此資料相關聯的唯一 EUII 是 C1 的電子郵件地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-810">The only EUII associated with this data is an email address of the C1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-811">此地址為傳送新預約通知和更新電子郵件的目標。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-811">This address is where new booking notifications and update emails are sent.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p247">**客戶連絡人：** 在 Bookings Web、iOS 及 Android 用戶端中可以手動建立連絡人，也可以從行動裝置進行匯入。在使用自助式預約頁面期間也會自動建立連絡人。其包含 EUII 並儲存在 Bookings 信箱中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p247">**Customer contacts:** Contacts can be manually created in the Bookings Web, iOS, and Android clients, or they can be imported from a mobile device. Contacts are also automatically created during the use of the self-service booking page. They contain EUII and are stored in the Bookings mailbox.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p248">**員工詳細資料：** 客戶內容包括有資格提供從 Bookings Web、iOS 或 Android 用戶端建立之服務的員工相關資料。員工詳細資料可以包含名稱、電子郵件地址和電話號碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p248">**Staff details:** Customer content includes data about the staff that are eligible to deliver the services created from either the Bookings Web, iOS, or Android clients. Staff details can contain name, email address, and phone number.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p249">**預約事件：** 這些是企業使用 Web 用戶端或 Android/iOS 應用程式所建立，或由客戶使用公用預約頁面 (或 Facebook 頁面) 所建立的客戶會議和相關客戶內容。這些事件可以包括名稱、地址、電子郵件地址、電話號碼及約會詳細資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p249">**Booking events:** These are customer meetings and related customer content created by the business using a Web client or Android/iOS app, or created by the customer using a public booking page (or a Facebook page). These events can include name, address, email address, phone number, and appointment details.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p250">**會議要求、電子郵件確認/取消/更新，以及電子郵件提醒：** 這些是由系統傳送的預約相關電子郵件訊息。其中包含在預約時輸入的員工資料和客戶資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p250">**Meeting requests, email confirmations/cancellations/updates, and email reminders:** These are email messages sent by the system in association with bookings. They contain staff data and customer data that was entered at time of booking.</span></span>

##### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-821">匯出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-821">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-822">若要匯出企業主、員工和客戶的對應資料，您可以使用[商務中心隱私權入口網站](https://businessaccount.microsoft.com/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-822">To export data corresponding to the business owner, staff and customers, you can use the [Business center privacy portal](https://businessaccount.microsoft.com/).</span></span>

##### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-823">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-823">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-824">您可以刪除下列類型的 Bookings 資料，以回應 DSR 刪除要求：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-824">You can delete the following types of Bookings data in response to a DSR deleting request:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-825">**企業設定檔資訊和連絡人：** 您可以在系統管理中心刪除 Bookings 信箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-825">**Business profile information and contacts:** You can delete the Bookings mailbox in the admin center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-826">刪除信箱之後，您可以在 30 天內將它還原。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-826">After you delete the mailbox, you can restore it with 30 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-827">30 天之後，就會永久刪除帳戶和對應的信箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-827">After 30 days, the account and the corresponding mailbox are permanently deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-828">如需刪除使用者帳戶的詳細資訊，請參閱[刪除使用者](#deleting-a-user)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-828">For details about deleting a user account, see the section [Deleting a user](#deleting-a-user).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p252">**員工詳細資料：** 您可以從 Bookings 儀表板中刪除員工。若要永久刪除員工，您可以刪除其 Office 365 帳戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p252">**Staff details:** You can delete staff from the Bookings dashboard. To permanently detail staff, you can delete their Office 365 account.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-831">**Bookings 事件：** 您可以從 Bookings 行事曆中刪除 Bookings 事件，這會移除客戶的資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-831">**Bookings events:** You can delete bookings events from the Bookings calendar, which will remove the customer's information.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-832">**會議要求、電子郵件確認/取消/更新以及電子郵件提醒：** 您可以從 Bookings 行事曆中刪除這些項目，這會移除客戶的資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-832">**Meeting requests, email confirmations/cancellations/updates, and email reminders:** You can delete these from the Bookings calendar, which will remove the customer's information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-833">若要匯出企業主、員工和客戶的對應資料，您可以使用[商務中心隱私權入口網站](https://businessaccount.microsoft.com/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-833">To export data corresponding to the business owner, staff and customers, you can use the [Business center privacy portal](https://businessaccount.microsoft.com/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p253">此外，您可以刪除企業主和員工資料，也可以刪除對應的使用者帳戶。請參閱[刪除使用者](#deleting-a-user)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p253">Additionally, you can delete business owner and staff data, you can delete the corresponding user account. See the section  [Deleting a user](#deleting-a-user).</span></span>

#### <a name="listings"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-836">Listings</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-836">Listings</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-837">下列各節說明如何使用 Microsoft Listings 中的應用程式內功能，來尋找、存取、匯出及刪除個人資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-837">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Listings to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

##### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-838">探索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-838">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p254">Listings 擁有者可以將其企業連線至 Google、Bing、Yelp，以查看評分和評論的匯總檢視。Listings 會收集並儲存下列類型的資料：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p254">Listings owner can connect their business to Google, Bing, Yelp, and Facebook to see an aggregated view of ratings and reviews. Listings collect and store the following types of data:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-841">Google 評論和評分</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-841">Google reviews and ratings</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-842">Bing 評論和評分</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-842">Bing reviews and ratings</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-843">Yelp 評論和評分</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-843">Yelp reviews and ratings</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-844">Facebook 評論和評分</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-844">Facebook reviews and ratings</span></span>

##### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-845">存取</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-845">Access</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="997d0-846">Listings 擁有者可以登入 Listings 儀表板來查看其評論和評分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-846">Listings owner can sign in to the Listings dashboard to see their reviews and ratings.</span></span>

##### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-847">匯出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-847">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-848">若要匯出企業主、員工和客戶的對應資料，您可以使用[商務中心隱私權入口網站](https://businessaccount.microsoft.com/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-848">To export data corresponding to the business owner, staff and customers, you can use the [Business center privacy portal](https://businessaccount.microsoft.com/).</span></span>

##### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-849">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-849">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p255">如果 Listings 擁有者想要刪除其 Listings 資訊，他們可以在 Listings 頁面上中斷與提供者的連線。在他們中斷連線之後，就會刪除其 Listings 資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p255">If a Listings owner would like to delete their Listings information, they can disconnect from the provider on the Listings page. After they disconnect, their Listings information will be deleted.</span></span>

#### <a name="connections"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-852">連線</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-852">Connections</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-853">下列各節說明如何使用 Microsoft Connections 中的應用程式內功能，來尋找、存取、匯出及刪除個人資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-853">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Connections to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

##### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-854">探索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-854">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-855">Connections 會收集並儲存下列類型的資料：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-855">Connections collect and store the following types of data:</span></span> 

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p256">客戶/連絡人是由企業使用 Web 用戶端或行動裝置應用程式 (iOS、Android) 建立，或在商務連絡人收到電子郵件行銷活動時使用應用程式建立。客戶資料可以包括名稱、地址、電子郵件地址及稅務識別碼。所有商務中心應用程式會共用連絡人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p256">Customers/contacts are created by the business using the web client or mobile app (iOS, Android), or by using the app when a business contact is sent an email marketing campaign. Customer data can include name, address, email address, and tax ID numbers. Contacts are shared across all Business center apps.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-859">客戶可以在 Connections 註冊頁面上進行註冊，並儲存其個人資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-859">Customers can sign up on the Connections sign-up page and save their personal information.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-860">電子郵件行銷活動中的連結</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-860">Links from email campaigns</span></span>

##### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-861">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-861">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-862">Connections 擁有者可以登入 Connections 儀表板，並查看他們所傳送的電子郵件行銷活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-862">A Connections owner can sign in to the Connections dashboard and see the email campaigns they've sent.</span></span>

##### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-863">匯出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-863">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-864">若要匯出企業主、員工和客戶的對應資料，您可以使用[商務中心隱私權入口網站](https://businessaccount.microsoft.com/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-864">To export data corresponding to the business owner, staff and customers, you can use the [Business center privacy portal](https://businessaccount.microsoft.com/).</span></span>

##### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-865">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-865">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p257">在 Connections 擁有者傳送電子郵件行銷活動之後，就無法刪除該行銷活動。如果有他們想要刪除的草稿行銷活動，他們可以登入 Connections 儀表板並刪除草稿行銷活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p257">After a Connections owner sends an email campaign, they can't delete the campaign. If there are any draft campaigns they want to delete, they can sign in to the Connections dashboard and delete the draft campaigns.</span></span>

### <a name="education"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-868">Education</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-868">Education</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-869">本節說明如何使用下列 Microsoft 教育版應用程式的應用程式內功能來回應 DSR 要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-869">This section explains how to use the in-app functionality of the following Microsoft Education apps to respond to DSR requests.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-870">作業</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-870">Assignments</span></span>
