#### <a name="assignments"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-872">作業</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-872">Assignments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-873">下列各節說明如何使用「作業」中的應用程式內功能，來尋找、存取、匯出及刪除個人資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-873">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Assignments to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

##### <a name="discoveraccess"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-874">探索/存取</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-874">Discover/Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p258">「作業」會儲存教師和學生所產生的資訊。其中有些資訊會儲存在 SharePoint 中，有些會儲存在非 SharePoint 位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p258">Assignments stores information that is generated both by teachers and students. Some of this information is store in SharePoint and some is stored in a non-SharePoint location.</span></span>

##### <a name="finding-assignments-data-stored-in-sharepoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-877">尋找 SharePoint 中儲存的「作業」資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-877">Finding Assignments data stored in SharePoint</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p259">與作業提交相關聯的學生檔案會儲存在文件庫 (名為 **學生功課**) 中，而與教師建立所建立且學生可存取的作業相關聯的檔案則會儲存在不同的文件庫 (名為 **課程檔案**) 中。這兩個文件庫都位於對應的課程小組 SharePoint 網站中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p259">Students files associated with a Submission for Assignment are stored in a document library (named **Student Work**) and files associated with Assignments that are created by teachers and (accessible by students) are stored in a different document library (named **Class Files**). Both document libraries are in the corresponding Class Team SharePoint site.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p260">系統管理員可以在安全性與合規性中心使用內容搜尋工具，搜尋與作業繳交情況相關的學生檔案 (在學生功課和課程檔案文件庫中)，以及與作業相關的檔案。例如，系統管理員可以搜尋組織中的所有 SharePoint 網站，並在搜尋查詢中使用學生的名稱、課程或作業名稱，以尋找與 DSR 要求相關的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p260">An admin can use the Content Search tool in the Security & Compliance Center to search for student files (in the Student Work and Class Files libraries) that are related to submissions on assignments and files related to assignments. For example, an admin could search all SharePoint sites in the organization and use the student's name and class or assignment name in the search query to find data relevant to a DSR request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p261">同樣地，系統管理員可以搜尋作業相關教師檔案中教師派給學生的檔案。例如，系統管理員可以搜尋組織中的所有 SharePoint 網站，並在搜尋查詢中使用教師的名稱、課程或作業名稱，以尋找與 DSR 要求相關的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p261">Similarly, an admin can search for teacher files related to assignments for files that a teacher distributed to students. For example, an admin could search all SharePoint sites in the organization and use the teacher's name and class or assignment name in the search query to find data relevant to a DSR request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-884">如需詳細資訊，請參閱：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-884">For more information, see:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-885">作業系統管理員文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-885">Assignments Admin Documentation</span></span>](/microsoft-365/education/deploy/assignments-admin-documentation)
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-886">[使用內容搜尋電子文件探索工具來回應 DSR](#using-the-content-search-ediscovery-tool-to-respond-to-dsrs) (本指南中)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-886">[Using the Content Search eDiscovery tool to respond to DSRs](#using-the-content-search-ediscovery-tool-to-respond-to-dsrs) (in this guide)</span></span>

##### <a name="finding-assignments-data-not-stored-in-sharepoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-887">尋找未儲存在 SharePoint 中的「作業」資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-887">Finding Assignments data not stored in SharePoint</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p262">下列類型的「作業」資料不會儲存在課程小組 SharePoint 網站中，因此無法使用內容搜尋來探索。此資料包括下列各項：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p262">The following types of Assignments data are not stored in the class team SharePoint site, and therefore aren't discoverable by using Content Search. This data this includes the following:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-890">學生的成績和老師的意見反應</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-890">Student grades and feedback from the teacher</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-891">每個學生針對作業所提交的文件清單</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-891">The list of documents submitted for an assignment by each student</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-892">作業詳細資料，例如作業到期的日期</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-892">Assignment details, like the date the assignment is due</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p263">若要尋找的資料，系統管理員或教師必須進入課程小組網站中的 [作業]，以找出可能與 DSR 要求相關的資料。系統管理員可以將本身新增為課程的擁有者，並檢視該課程小組的所有作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p263">To find data, an admin or a teacher would have to go into the Assignment in the Class Team site to find data that may be relevant to a DSR request. An admin can add themselves as an owner to the class and view all the assignments for that class team.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p264">即使學生已經不屬於某個課程，其資料仍可能出現在課程中並標示為「不再是註冊學生」。在此情況下，提交 DSR 要求的學生必須將他們正式註冊的課程清單提供給系統管理員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p264">Even if a student is no longer part of a class, their data might still be present in the class and marked as "no longer enrolled". In this case, a student submitting a DSR request would have to provide the admin the list of classes that they were formally enrolled it.</span></span>

##### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-897">匯出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-897">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p265">您可以使用 PowerShell 指令碼取得學生的課程清單，然後使用 PowerShell 指令碼匯出資料，來匯出特定學生已註冊之所有課程的作業資料。請參閲：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p265">You can export Assignments data for a specific student for all classes in which the student is enrolled by using a PowerShell script to get a list of classes for the student and then using a PowerShell script to export the data. See:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-900">設定 Teams 作業</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-900">Configure Assignments for Teams</span></span>](/microsoft-365/education/deploy/configure-assignments-for-teams)
- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-901">取得特定學生的課程清單</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-901">Get a list of classes for a specific student</span></span>](/microsoft-365/education/deploy/assignments-script-get)
- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-902">從「作業」中匯出學生和教師資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-902">Export student and teacher data from Assignments</span></span>](/microsoft-365/education/deploy/assignments-script-export)

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p266">如果已從課程小組網站中移除此學生，系統管理員可以在執行匯出指令碼前，先將學生新增回該網站。或者，系統管理員可以使用指令碼的輸入檔，找出學生曾經註冊的每個課程。您也可以使用「作業」匯出指令碼來匯出教師有權存取之所有作業的提交資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p266">If the student has been removed from the Team Class site, the admin can add the student back to the site before running the export script. Or the admin can use the input file for the script to identify every class that the student was ever enrolled in. You can also use the Assignment export script to export submissions data for all assignments that a teacher has access to.</span></span>

##### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-906">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-906">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-907">您可以使用 PowerShell 指令碼取得學生的課程清單，然後使用 PowerShell 指令碼刪除資料，來刪除特定學生已註冊之所有課程的作業資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-907">You can delete Assignments data for a specific student for all classes in which the student is enrolled by using a PowerShell script to get a list of classes for the student and then using a PowerShell script to delete the data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-908">您應在從課程中移除學生之前這麼做。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-908">You should do this before you remove the student from the class.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-909">請參閱：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-909">See:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-910">設定 Teams 作業</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-910">Configure Assignments for Teams</span></span>](/microsoft-365/education/deploy/configure-assignments-for-teams)
- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-911">取得特定學生的課程清單</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-911">Get a list of classes for a specific student</span></span>](/microsoft-365/education/deploy/assignments-script-get)
- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-912">從「作業」中刪除學生資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-912">Delete student data from Assignments</span></span>](/microsoft-365/education/deploy/assignments-script-delete)

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p268">如果已從課程小組網站中移除此學生，系統管理員可以在執行匯出指令碼前，先將學生新增回該網站。或者，系統管理員可以使用指令碼的輸入檔，找出學生曾經註冊的每個課程。您無法使用「作業」刪除指令碼來刪除教師資料，因為在課程小組網站中會共用所有的作業。此外，系統管理員必須將本身新增至課程小組，然後刪除特定作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p268">If the student has been removed from the Team Class site, the admin can add the student back to the site before running the export script. Or the admin can use the input file for the script to identify every class that the student was ever enrolled in. You can't use the Assignments deletion script to delete teacher data because all Assignments are shared across the Class Team site. As an alternative, an admin would have to add themselves to the Class Team site and then delete a specific Assignment.</span></span>

#### <a name="class-notebook"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-917">課程筆記本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-917">Class Notebook</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-918">稍早已在本指南中討論如何在課程筆記本中搜尋內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-918">Searching for content in Class Notebook is discussed previously in this guide.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-919">請參閱 [OneNote 課程筆記本](#onenote-class-notebook)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-919">See the [OneNote Class Notebook](#onenote-class-notebook) section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-920">您也可以使用「 內容搜尋 」工具匯出課程筆記本中的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-920">You can also use the Content Search tool to export data from a Class Notebook.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-921">此外，系統管理員或資料主體也可以匯出課程筆記本中的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-921">Alternatively, an admin or the data subject can export data from a Class Notebook.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-922">請參閱[儲存課程筆記本複本](https://support.office.com/article/44733e18-0ef1-4d4b-be51-fc2ac5bfe9ec)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-922">See [Save a copy of a Class Notebook](https://support.office.com/article/44733e18-0ef1-4d4b-be51-fc2ac5bfe9ec).</span></span>

### <a name="flow"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-923">Flow</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-923">Flow</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-924">下列各節說明如何使用 Microsoft Flow 中的應用程式內功能，來尋找、存取、匯出及刪除個人資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-924">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Flow to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-925">探索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-925">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p270">人員可以使用 Flow 來執行資料相關工作，例如同步處理應用程式之間的檔案、將某個 Office 365 服務中的檔案複製到另一個服務，以及從某個 Office 365 應用程式中收集資料，並將其儲存在另一個服務中。例如，使用者可設定一個 Flow，以將 Outlook 電子郵件附件儲存至其商務用 OneDrive 帳戶。在此範例中，您可以使用「內容搜尋」工具來搜尋使用者信箱，以找出包含附件的電子郵件訊息，或搜尋其商務用 OneDrive 帳戶，以找出檔案。在以下範例中，您可在 Flow 工作流程所連接的 Office 365 服務中，探索 Flow 所處理的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p270">People can use Flow to perform data-related tasks such as synchronizing files between applications, copying files from one Office 365 service to another, and collecting data from one Office 365 app and storing it in another. For example, a user could set up a Flow to save Outlook email attachments to their OneDrive for Business account. In this example, you could use the Content Search tool to search the user's mailbox for the email message that contained the attachment or search their OneDrive for Business account for the file. This is an example where data handled by Flow might be discoverable in the Office 365 services connected by a Flow workflow.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p271">此外，人員可以使用 Flow，將 Office 365 中的檔案複製或上傳至外部服務，例如 Dropbox。在這些情況下，有關外部服務中資料的 DSR 要求必須提交給外部服務；因為在這類案例中是由外部服務來處理這些資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p271">Additionally, people can use Flow to copy or upload files from Office 365 to an external service, such as Dropbox. In these cases, a DSR request concerning the data in an external service would have to be submitted to the external service, who is processing the data in this type of scenario.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-932">如果系統管理員收到 DSR 要求，可以將自己新增為使用者流程的擁有者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-932">If an admin receives a DSR request, they can add themselves as an owner of a user's flows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-933">這可讓系統管理員執行匯出流程定義、執行歷程記錄，以及執行流程權限重新指派等功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-933">This enables an admin to perform functions including exporting flow definitions, running histories, and performing flow permission reassignments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-934">請參閱[管理系統管理中心內的流程](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/managing-flow-resources-in-the-admin-center/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-934">See [Manage Flows in the Admin Center](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/managing-flow-resources-in-the-admin-center/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-935">系統管理員需要具有下列權限的帳戶，才能夠將自己新增為 Flow 的擁有者：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-935">An admin's ability to add themselves as an owner of a Flow requires an account with the following permissions:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-936">Flow/PowerApps 方案 2 授權 (付費或試用版)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-936">Flow/PowerApps Plan 2 license (paid or trial)</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-937">全域系統管理員\ </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-937">Global administrator\ </span></span>](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/assign-admin-roles)

    <span data-ttu-id="997d0-938">或</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-938">or</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-939">Azure Active Directory 全域系統管理員</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-939">Azure Active Directory global administrator</span></span>](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles-azure-portal)

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-940">要具有這些權限，才可讓系統管理員使用 Flow 系統管理中心存取組織中的所有流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-940">Having these privileges enables the admin to use the Flow admin center to access all Flows in the organization.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-941">若要將自己新增為流程的擁有者：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-941">To add yourself as an owner of a flow.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-942">請移至 <https://admin.flow.microsoft.com></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-942">Go to <https://admin.flow.microsoft.com></span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-943">使用您的 Office 365 認證來登入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-943">Sign in with your Office 365 credentials.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-944">在 [環境 **]** 頁面上，選取您想要存取之流程的環境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-944">On the **Environments** page, select the environment for the flows that you want to access.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-945">組織會有預設的環境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-945">organizations have a default environment.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-946">在所選環境的頁面上，選取 [資源 **]**，然後選取 [流程 **]**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-946">On the page for the environment that you selected, select **Resources**, and then select **Flows.**</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-947">環境中所有流程的清單隨即顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-947">A list of all flows in the environment is displayed.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-948">針對您想要將自己新增為其成員的流程，選取 [檢視詳細資料 **]**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-948">select **View details** for the flow that you want to add yourself as a member.</span></span>
6. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-949">在 [擁有者 **]** 底下，選取 [管理共用 **]**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-949">Under **Owners**, select **Manage sharing**.</span></span>
7. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-950">在 [共用 **]** 飛出視窗中，將您自己新增為成員，然後儲存變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-950">On the **Share** flyout, add yourself as a member and then save the change.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p275">在使自己成為擁有者之後，請移至 **[流程]** \>**[我的流程]** \> **[小組流程]**，來存取流程。您可以從那裡下載執行歷程記錄或匯出流程。請參閱：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p275">After you make yourself an owner, go to **Flow** \> **My flows** \> **Team flows** to access the flow. From there, you can download the run history or export the flow. See:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-954">下載流程執行歷程記錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-954">Download flow run history</span></span>](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/download-history-recurrence/)
- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-955">使用封裝跨環境匯出和匯入您的流程</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-955">Export and import your flows across environments with packaging</span></span>](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/import-export-bap-packages/)

#### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-956">存取</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-956">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-957">使用者可以存取其流程的定義和執行歷程記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-957">A user can access the definitions and run histories of their flows.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-958">**流程定義：** 使用者可以匯出流程的定義 (將其匯出為流程套件，並以壓縮檔案形式格式化為 JSON)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-958">**Flow definitions:** A user can export the definition of a flow (which is exported as a Flow package, formatted as JSON in a zipped file).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-959">請參閱[使用封裝跨環境匯出和匯入您的流程](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/import-export-bap-packages/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-959">See [Export and import your flows across environments with packaging](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/import-export-bap-packages/).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-960">**流程執行歷程記錄：** 使用者可下載其各個流程的執行歷程記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-960">**Flow run histories:** A user can download the run history of each of their flows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-961">流程執行歷程記錄下載格式為 CSV 檔案，可在 Excel 中開啟進行篩選或搜尋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-961">A flow run history is downloaded as a CSV file, which can be opened in Excel to filter or search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-962">使用者也可以下載多個流程的執行歷程記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-962">Users can also download the run history of multiple flows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-963">請參閱[下載流程執行歷程記錄](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/download-history-recurrence/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-963">See [Download flow run history](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/download-history-recurrence/).</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-964">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-964">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p278">系統管理員可在 Flow 系統管理中心，將自己新增為使用者的流程的擁有者。當使用者從貴組織離職且其 Office 365 帳戶遭到刪除，該使用者是唯一擁有者的流程仍會保留。這是為了協助貴組織將流程移轉給新的擁有者，並避免因無法共用業務流程的應用程式而造成業務中斷。然後，系統管理員必須決定要刪除使用者所擁有的流程，還是只重新指派給新的擁有者，並採取該動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p278">An admin can add themselves as an owner of a user's flows in the Flow admin center. If a user leaves your organization and their Office 365 account is deleted, the flows that they are the sole owner of will be retained. This is to help your organization transition the flows to new owners and avoid any disruption to your business for flows that may be used for shared business processes. An admin then needs to determine whether to delete the flows that were owned by the user or reassign to new owners, and take that action.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-969">若為共用流程，使用者從貴組織刪除時，其名稱也會從擁有者清單中移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-969">For shared flows, when a user is deleted from your organization, their name is removed from the list of owners.</span></span>

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-970">匯出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-970">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p279">系統管理員可以匯出使用者流程的定義和執行歷程記錄。若要這樣做，系統管理員必須在 Flow 系統管理中心，將自己新增為使用者流程的擁有者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p279">An admin can export the definition and run history of a user's flows. To do this, an admin must add themselves as an owner of the user's flow in the Flow admin center</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-973">**流程定義：** 在系統管理員將自己新增為流程的擁有者後，可以移至 **[流程]** \>**[我的流程]** \> **[小組流程]**，來匯出流程定義 (將其匯出為流程套件，並以壓縮檔案形式格式化為 JSON)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-973">**Flow definitions:** After an admin adds themselves as an owner of a flow, they can go to **Flow** \> **My Flows** \> **Teams flows** to export the flow definition (which is exported as a Flow package, formatted as JSON in a zipped file).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-974">請參閱[使用封裝跨環境匯出和匯入您的流程](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/import-export-bap-packages/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-974">See [Export and import your flows across environments with packaging](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/import-export-bap-packages/).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-975">**流程執行記錄：** 同樣地，系統管理員必須將自己新增為流程的擁有者，才能匯出流程執行歷程記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-975">**Flow run histories:** Similarly, an admin must add themselves as an owner of a Flow to export its flow run history.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-976">流程執行歷程記錄下載格式為 CSV 檔案，這表示您可使用 Excel 進行篩選或搜尋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-976">The Flow run history is downloaded as a CSV file, which means you can use Excel to filter or search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-977">只要您具有擁有全，也可下載多個流程的執行歷程記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-977">You can also download the run history of multiple Flows, as long as you have ownership.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-978">請參閱[下載流程執行歷程記錄](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/download-history-recurrence/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-978">See [Download flow run history](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/download-history-recurrence/).</span></span>

#### <a name="connections-and-custom-connectors-in-flow"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-979">Flow 中的 Connections 和自訂連接器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-979">Connections and custom connectors in Flow</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p282">[連線] 需要使用者提供認證，才能連線至 API、SaaS 應用程式，以及自訂開發系統。這些連線由建立連線的使用者所擁有，並可在產品內[管理](/flow/add-manage-connections)。在重新指派 Flows 之後，系統管理員可以使用 PowerShell Cmdlet，在刪除使用者資料的過程中列出並刪除這些連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p282">Connections require users to provide credentials to connect to APIs, SaaS applications, and custom developed systems. These connections are owned by the user that established the connection and can be [managed](/flow/add-manage-connections) in-product. After Flows have been reassigned, an admin can use PowerShell cmdlets to list and delete these connections as part of deleting user data.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p283">自訂連接器可讓組織連線至現成連接器無法使用的系統，來擴充 Flow 的功能。自訂連接器作者可將其連接器與組織中的其他人[共用](/flow/register-custom-api)。在收到 DSR 刪除要求後，系統管理員應該考慮重新指派這些連接器的擁有權，以避免業務中斷。若要加快此程序，系統管理員可以使用 PowerShell Cmdlet，來列出、重新指派或刪除自訂連接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p283">Custom connectors allow organizations to extend the capabilities of Flow by connecting to systems where an out-of-box connector is not available. A custom connector author can [share](/flow/register-custom-api) their connector with others in an organization. After receiving a DSR deleting request, an admin should consider reassigning ownership of these connectors to avoid business disruption. To expedite this process, an admin can use PowerShell cmdlets to list, reassign, or delete custom connectors.</span></span>

### <a name="forms"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-987">Forms</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-987">Forms</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-988">下列各節說明如何使用 Microsoft Forms 中的應用程式內功能，來尋找、存取、匯出及刪除個人資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-988">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Forms to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-989">探索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-989">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p284">Forms 使用者可以移至 <https://forms.office.com>，然後選取 [我的表單]，以查看他們所建立的 Forms。他們也可以選取 [與我共用]，來檢視其他人透過連結所共用的 Forms。如果有許多要排序的 Forms，使用者可以使用產品內搜尋列，依標題或作者搜尋 Forms。若要判斷 Microsoft Forms 是否為可回應 DSR 的個人資料所在的位置，您可以要求資料主體搜尋其 [與我共用] 清單，來判斷哪些使用者 (「Forms 擁有者」) 已將 Forms 傳送給資料主體。然後，您可以要求表單擁有者選取導覽列上方的 [共用]，並將特定表單的連結傳送給您，讓您可以檢視，並進一步判斷該表單對 DSR 是否重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p284">Forms users can go to <https://forms.office.com> and select **My forms** to see the Forms they've created. They can also select **Shared with me** to view Forms others have shared via a link. If there are many Forms to sort through, users can use the in-product search bar to search for Forms by title or author. To determine whether Microsoft Forms is a place where personal data responsive to your DSR is likely to reside, you can ask the Data Subject to search his or her **Shared with me** list to determine which users ("Forms owners") have sent Forms to the Data Subject. You can then ask the forms owners to select **Share** in the top navigation bar and send you a link to a specific form so you can view it and further determine whether it is material to your DSR.</span></span>

#### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-995">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-995">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-996">在找到相關的 Forms 之後，您可以按一下 [回應 **]** 索引標籤，來存取表單的回應。深入了解如何 [檢查您的測驗結果](https://support.microsoft.com/office/check-and-share-your-quiz-results-c4a9b45c-d62f-4eb7-b5db-ad81892c7c07)或 [表單結果](https://support.office.com/article/02859424-341d-406f-b32a-9a0fbaf357af)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-996">After the relevant Forms are found, you can access the responses to the Form by clicking the **Responses** tab. Learn more about how to [check your quiz results](https://support.microsoft.com/office/check-and-share-your-quiz-results-c4a9b45c-d62f-4eb7-b5db-ad81892c7c07) or [form results](https://support.office.com/article/02859424-341d-406f-b32a-9a0fbaf357af).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-997">若要在 Excel 中檢閱回應結果，請選取 [回應 **]** 索引標籤，然後選取 [在 Excel 中開啟 **]**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-997">To review response results in Excel, select the **Responses** tab, and then select **Open in Excel**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-998">如果您想要將表單的複本傳送給資料主體，則可以取得以 RTF 格式顯示在應用程式中之相關問答的螢幕擷取畫面，或將結果的 Excel 複本傳送給資料主體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-998">If you would like to send the Data Subject a copy of the Form, you can either take screenshots of the relevant questions and answers that are in shown in the application in rich text format or send the Data Subject an Excel copy of the results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-999">如果您正在使用 Excel，且只想要與資料主體共用問卷結果的一部分，可以刪除特定列或欄，或刪減剩餘的區段，然後共用結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-999">If you are using Excel and would like to share with the Data Subject only portions of the survey result, you can delete certain rows or columns or redact the remaining sections before sharing the results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1000">或者，您也可以移至 [共用]**\> [取得複製的連結]** (在 [共用] 下的範本)，以便將整個表單的複寫提供給資料主體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1000">Alternatively, you can go to **Share \> Get a link to duplicate** (under Share as a template) to provide the Data Subject with a replicate of the entire Form.</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1001">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1001">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1002">任何問卷、測驗、問卷調查或投票可由其擁有者永久刪除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1002">Any survey, quiz, questionnaire, or poll can be permanently deleted by its owner.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1003">如果您想要接受「忘記我」DSR 並刪除整個表單，請尋找表單清單中的表單、在表單預覽視窗右上角選取一連串的點 (省略符號)，然後選取 [刪除 **]**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1003">If you would like to honor a DSR "forget me" and delete a form in its entirety, find the Form in the list of forms, select the series of dots (ellipsis) in the upper right corner of the form preview window, and then select **Delete**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1004">表單一經刪除，便無法擷取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1004">Once a Form is deleted, it can't be retrieved.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1005">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[刪除表單](https://support.microsoft.com/office/delete-a-form-2207e468-ce1b-4c4a-a256-caf631d87af0)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1005">For information, see [Delete a Form](https://support.microsoft.com/office/delete-a-form-2207e468-ce1b-4c4a-a256-caf631d87af0).</span></span>

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1006">匯出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1006">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1007">若要將表單問題和回應匯出至 Excel 檔案，請開啟表單、選取 [回應] 索引標籤，然後選取 [在 Excel 中開啟]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1007">To export form questions and responses to an Excel file, open the form, select the **Responses** tab, and then select **Open in Excel**.</span></span>

### <a name="kaizala"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1008">Kaizala</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1008">Kaizala</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1009">下列各節說明如何使用 Microsoft Kaizala 中的應用程式內功能，來尋找、存取、匯出及刪除個人資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1009">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Kaizala to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1010">探索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1010">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p287">系統管理員可從 Kaizala 管理入口網站存取使用者的組織資料 (也就是在組織群組共用的資料)。組織資料的保留期間是由貴組織的保留原則所決定。除了使用者資料，Kaizala 伺服器也會儲存下列類型的組織資料：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p287">A user's organizational data, which is data that is shared in organizational groups, can be accessed by an admin from the Kaizala management portal. Organizational data is retained for a duration of time determined by your organization's retention policies. In addition to user data, Kaizala servers also store the following types of organizational data:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1014">屬於組織群組的成員清單</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1014">List of members who are part of the organization's groups</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1015">組織群組訊息資料，也就是整個組織群組共用的訊息和回應</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1015">Organization group messages data, which are messages and responses shared across organizational groups</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1016">組織中的使用者清單</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1016">A list of users in the organizations</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1017">針對組織中所有使用者擷取的產品和服務使用情況資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1017">Product and service usage data captured for all users in the organization.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1018">組織所建立的 Kaizala 動作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1018">Kaizala Actions created by the organization</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1019">Kaizala 連接器資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1019">Kaizala connectors data</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p288">資料主體可以使用適用於消費者資料的 Kaizala 行動裝置應用程式來存取使用者的消費者資料。消費者資料包括下列類型的資料：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p288">A user's consumer data can be accessed by the data subject using the Kaizala mobile app for consumer data. Consumer data includes the following types of data:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1022">屬於 Kaizala 上私人群組的資料 (儲存在 Kaizala 伺服器上 90 天)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1022">Data belonging to private groups on Kaizala (stored on Kaizala servers for 90 days)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1023">使用者的設定檔資訊，以及使用者的連絡人</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1023">A user's profile information and the user's contacts</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1024">與使用者屬於相同群組的成員清單</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1024">List of members who are part of the same groups as the user</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1025">各群組共用的群組訊息和回應</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1025">Group messages and responses shared across groups</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1026">使用者的連絡人清單 (儲存於 Kaizala 服務)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1026">The user's contact list (stored on Kaizala service)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1027">使用者在 Kaizala 上所進行的交易 (僅適用於印度的 Kaizala 使用者)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1027">Transactions made by the user on Kaizala (applies to Kaizala users in India only)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1028">使用者的產品和服務使用情況資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1028">Product and service usage data for the user</span></span>

#### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1029">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1029">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p289">Kaizala 使用者可以移至其行動裝置，查看他們在其裝置上所建立的 Kaizala 內容。若要判斷 Kaizala 行動裝置應用程式是否為可回應 DSR 的個人資料的所在位置，您可以要求資料主體在其 Kaizala 應用程式中搜尋所要求的資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p289">Kaizala users can go to their mobile device to see Kaizala content they've created on their device. To determine whether Kaizala mobile apps are a place where personal data responsive to a DSR is likely to reside, you can ask the data subject to search their Kaizala app for the requested information.</span></span>

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1032">匯出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1032">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p290">當貴組織中的使用者使用 Kaizala 時，就會產生消費者資料，而如果使用者參與組織群組，則可能會產生組織資料。系統管理員可以從 Kaizala 管理入口網站匯出使用者的組織資料。Kaizala 消費者使用者可以從 Kaizala 行動裝置應用程式匯出其私人資料。在這兩種情況下，請注意，當系統管理員或使用者匯出 Kaizala 資料時，也會匯出產品和服務使用情況資料。如需詳細資訊，請參閱：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p290">When users in your organization use Kaizala, consumer data is generated, and organizational data may be generated if the user participates in an organization group. Admins can export a user's organizational data from the Kaizala management portal. Kaizala consumer users can export their private data from the Kaizala mobile app. In both cases, note that product and service usage data is also export when an admin or user exports Kaizala data. For details, see:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1038">在 Kaizala 中匯出或刪除使用者的組織資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1038">Export or delete a user's organizational data in Kaizala</span></span>](/office365/kaizala/export-or-delete-a-user-s-data)
- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1039">在 Kaizala 行動應用程式中匯出或刪除您的資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1039">Export or delete your data in the Kaizala mobile app</span></span>](/office365/kaizala/export-or-delete-your-data)

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1040">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1040">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p291">Kaizala 系統管理員可以在 Kaizala 管理入口網站中移除 Kaizala 使用者的帳戶。刪除使用者帳戶之後，就會從屬於貴組織的所有群組中移除使用者，並從他們的裝置中刪除組織資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p291">A Kaizala admin can remove a Kaizala user's account in the Kaizala management portal. After a user account is deleted, the user is removed from all groups that belong to your organization and organizational data is deleted from their device.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p292">若要從使用者的行動裝置移除所有私人資料，Kaizala 使用者可以刪除其 Kaizala 帳戶。刪除帳戶之後，就會從裝置中刪除所有相關的 Kaizala 內容，包括聊天、相片和其他資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p292">To remove all private data from the user's mobile device, the Kaizala user can delete their Kaizala account. After the account is deleted, all related Kaizala content including, chats, photos, and other data will be deleted from the device.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1045">如需詳細資訊，請參閱：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1045">For details, see:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1046">在 Kaizala 中匯出或刪除使用者的組織資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1046">Export or delete a user's organizational data in Kaizala</span></span>](/office365/kaizala/export-or-delete-a-user-s-data)
- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1047">在 Kaizala 行動應用程式中匯出或刪除您的資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1047">Export or delete your data in the Kaizala mobile app</span></span>](/office365/kaizala/export-or-delete-your-data)

### <a name="planner"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1048">Planner</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1048">Planner</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1049">下列各節說明如何使用 Microsoft Planner 中的應用程式內功能，來尋找、存取、匯出及刪除個人資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1049">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Planner to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1050">探索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1050">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1051">Planner 計劃與 Microsoft 365 群組相關聯，而且 Microsoft 365 群組的檔案會儲存在該群組的相關聯 SharePoint Online 網站中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1051">Planner plans are associated with a Microsoft 365 Group, and the files for Microsoft 365 Groups are stored in an associated SharePoint Online site for the group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1052">這表示您可以使用內容搜尋來搜尋 Microsoft 365 群組的網站，以尋找 Planner 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1052">That means that you can use Content Search to find Planner files by searching the site for the Microsoft 365 Group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1053">若要這麼做，您必須要有 Microsoft 365 群組的 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1053">To do this, you need to have the URL for the Microsoft 365 Group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1054">如需如何取得 Microsoft 365 群組之相關資訊的提示，請參閱「Office 365 中的內容搜尋」說明主題中的[搜尋 Microsoft Teams 和 Microsoft 365 群組](/microsoft-365/compliance/content-search)，來協助您在對應的 SharePoint Online 網站中搜尋 Planner 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1054">See [Searching Microsoft Teams and Microsoft 365 Groups](/microsoft-365/compliance/content-search) in the "Content Search in Office 365" help topic for tips about getting information about Microsoft 365 Groups to help you search for Planner files in the corresponding SharePoint Online site.</span></span>

#### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1055">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1055">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p294">如先前所述，您可以搜尋與計劃相關聯的基礎 SharePoint Online 網站和信箱。然後，您可以預覽或下載相關的搜尋結果來存取資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p294">As previously explained, you can search the underlying SharePoint Online site and mailbox that are associated with a plan. Then you can preview or download the related search results to access data.</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1058">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1058">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p295">您可以提供自己存取使用者所屬方案的權限，或以該使用者身分登入來進行變更，而手動刪除使用者的個人資訊。請參閱[刪除 Microsoft Planner 中的使用者資料](https://support.office.com/article/delete-user-data-in-microsoft-planner-4349ded2-1891-4896-8e27-05fd40f3929f)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p295">You can manually delete a user's personally information by either giving yourself permissions to access the plans the user is part of or signing in as the user to make the changes. See [Delete user data in Microsoft Planner](https://support.office.com/article/delete-user-data-in-microsoft-planner-4349ded2-1891-4896-8e27-05fd40f3929f).</span></span>

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1061">匯出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1061">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p296">您可以使用 PowerShell 指令碼，從 Planner 匯出使用者的資料。匯出資料時，會針對使用者所屬的每個計劃匯出 JSON 檔案。請參閱[從 Microsoft Planner 匯出使用者資料](https://support.office.com/article/export-user-data-from-microsoft-planner-91258c96-b353-4da1-b6d9-d78e4809cf08)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p296">You can use a PowerShell script to export a user's data from Planner. When you export the data, a separate JSON file is export for each plan that the user is a part of. See [Export user data from Microsoft Planner](https://support.office.com/article/export-user-data-from-microsoft-planner-91258c96-b353-4da1-b6d9-d78e4809cf08).</span></span>

### <a name="power-bi"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1065">Power BI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1065">Power BI</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1066">下列各節說明如何使用 Microsoft Power BI 中的應用程式內功能，來尋找、存取、匯出及刪除個人資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1066">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Power BI to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1067">探索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1067">Discover</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p297">您可以在 Power BI 中搜尋不同工作區中的內容，包括儀表板、報告、活頁簿和資料集。每種類型的工作區都包含一個搜尋欄位，您可用來搜尋該工作區。請參閱[在 Power BI 服務中搜尋、尋找及排序內容](/power-bi/service-navigation-search-filter-sort)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p297">You can search for content in the different workspaces in Power BI, including dashboards, reports, workbooks, and datasets. Each type of workspace contains a search field that you can use to search that workspace. See [Searching, finding, and sorting content in Power BI service](/power-bi/service-navigation-search-filter-sort).</span></span>

#### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1071">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1071">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1072">您可以從 Power BI 中的報告列印儀表板、報告及視覺效果，以取得實體複本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1072">You can print dashboards, reports, and visuals from reports in Power BI to produce a physical copy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1073">您無法列印整份報告；一次只能列印一頁。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1073">You can't print entire reports; you can only print one page at a time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1074">若要這麼做，請移至報告、使用搜尋欄位來尋找特定資料，然後列印該頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1074">To do this, go to a report, use the search field to find specific data, and then print that page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1075">請參閱[從 Power BI 服務中列印](/power-bi/service-print)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1075">See [Printing from Power BI service](/power-bi/service-print).</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1076">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1076">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1077">若要刪除儀表板、報告和活頁簿，請參閱[幾乎刪除 Power BI 服務中的一切](/power-bi/service-delete)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1077">To delete dashboards, reports, and workbooks, see [Delete almost anything in Power BI service](/power-bi/service-delete).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p299">刪除儀表板、報告或活頁簿並不會刪除基礎資料集。因為 Power BI 依賴與基礎來源資料的即時連線，才能完整且精確，所以必須在基礎來源資料中刪除個人資料。(例如，如果您建立了連線至 Dynamics 365 for Sales 的 Power BI 報告，作為即時資料來源，則您必須在 Dynamics 365 for Sales 中對資料進行所有更正。)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p299">Deleting a dashboard, report, or workbook doesn't delete the underlying dataset. Because Power BI relies on a live connection to the underlying source data to be complete and accurate, deleting personal data must be done there. (For example, if you created a Power BI report that is connected to Dynamics 365 for Sales as the live data source, you would have to make any corrections to the data in Dynamics 365 for Sales.)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1081">刪除資料之後，您可以使用 Power BI 中[排定的資料重新整理](/power-bi/refresh-scheduled-refresh)功能，來更新儲存在 Power BI 的資料集；在此之後，刪除的資料將不再反映在運用該資料的任何 Power BI 報告或儀表板中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1081">After the data is deleted, you can use the [scheduled data refresh](/power-bi/refresh-scheduled-refresh) capabilities in Power BI to update the dataset that is stored in Power BI, after which the deleted data will no longer be reflected in any Power BI reports or dashboards that used that data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1082">為了符合 GDPR 需求，您應該設有適當的原則，以確保能用適當的步調重新整理您的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1082">To help comply with GDPR requirements, you should have policies in place to ensure that you are refreshing your data at an appropriate cadence.</span></span>

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1083">匯出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1083">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1084">為了促成資料可攜性要求，您可以匯出 Power BI 中的儀表板和報告：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1084">To facilitate a data portability request, you can export dashboards and reports in Power BI:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p301">您可以將儀表板和報告的資料匯出至靜態 Excel 檔案。請參閱[從 Power BI 服務中列印](/power-bi/service-print)內的影片。然後，您可以使用 Excel，編輯要包含在可攜性要求中的個人資料，並以常用的、機器可讀取的格式 (例如 .csv 或 .xml) 來儲存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p301">You can export the underlying data for dashboards and reports to a static Excel file. See the video in [Printing from Power BI service](/power-bi/service-print). Using Excel, you can then edit the personal data to be included in the portability request, and save it in a commonly used, machine-readable format such as .csv or .xml.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p302">如果 Office 365 中的 Power BI 服務原先是用 Power BI Desktop 發佈的，您就可以從將報告匯出 (下載) 至 .pbix 檔案。然後，您可以將此檔案匯入至 Power BI Desktop，並發佈 (匯出) 至另一個組織的 Power BI 服務中。請參閱[將報告從 Power BI 服務匯出至 Desktop](/power-bi/service-export-to-pbix)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p302">You can export (download) a report from the Power BI service in Office 365 to a .pbix file if it was originally published using Power BI Desktop. You can then import this file to Power BI Desktop and publish (export) it to the Power BI service of another organization. See [Export a report from Power BI service to Desktop](/power-bi/service-export-to-pbix).</span></span>

### <a name="powerapps"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1091">PowerApps</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1091">PowerApps</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p303">下列各節說明如何使用 Microsoft Power Apps 中的應用程式內功能，來尋找、存取、匯出及刪除個人資料。下列步驟概述系統管理員如何將應用程式及其相關資源移轉給新的擁有者，以限制業務中斷。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p303">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Power Apps to find, access, export, and delete personal data. These steps outline how an admin can transition apps and their dependent resources to new owners to limit business disruption.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1094">探索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1094">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p304">PowerApps 是一種服務，用於組建可在貴組織內共用及使用的應用程式。在組建或執行應用程式時，使用者最終會將多種類型的資源和資料儲存在 PowerApps 服務中，包括應用程式、環境、連線、自訂連接器和權限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p304">PowerApps is a service for building apps that can be shared and used within your organization. As a part of the process of building or running an app, a user ends up storing several types of resources and data in the PowerApps service, including apps, environments, connections, custom connectors, and permissions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1097">若要促成與 PowerApps 相關的 DSR 要求，您可以運用 [PowerApps 系統管理中心](https://admin.powerapps.com/)和 [PowerApps Admin PowerShell Cmdlet](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871804) 中公開的系統管理作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1097">To help facilitate a DSR request related to PowerApps, you can use the administration operations exposed in the [PowerApps Admin Center](https://admin.powerapps.com/) and [PowerApps Admin PowerShell cmdlets](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871804).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1098">要存取這些工具將需要具有下列權限的帳戶：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1098">Access to these tools requires an account with the following permissions:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1099">付費的 PowerApps 方案 2 授權或 PowerApps 方案 2 試用版授權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1099">A paid PowerApps Plan 2 license or a PowerApps Plan 2 trial license.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1100">您可以在[這裡](https://web.powerapps.com/trial)註冊 30 天試用版授權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1100">You can sign up for a 30-day trial license [here](https://web.powerapps.com/trial).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1101">[全域系統管理員](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/assign-admin-roles)，或</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1101">[Global administrator](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/assign-admin-roles) or</span></span>
- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1102">Azure Active Directory 全域系統管理員</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1102">Azure Active Directory global administrator</span></span>](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles-azure-portal)

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1103">如需尋找個人資料的詳細資訊，請參閱[探索 PowerApps 個人資料](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871880)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1103">For more information about finding personal data, see [Discover PowerApps personal data](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871880).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1104">PowerApps 服務也包含了 Common Data Service For Apps，可讓使用者可以將資料儲存在 Common Data Service 資料庫內的標準和自訂實體中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1104">The PowerApps service also includes the Common Data Service For Apps, which enables users to store data in standard and custom entities within a Common Data Service database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1105">您可以從 [PowerApps Maker 入口網站](https://web.powerapps.com)中檢視儲存在這些實體中的資料，並使用[進階尋找](/dynamics365/customer-engagement/basics/save-advanced-find-search)的產品內搜尋功能，來搜尋實體中的特定資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1105">You can view the data stored in these entities from the [PowerApps Maker portal](https://web.powerapps.com), and use the in-product search capabilities of [Advanced Find](/dynamics365/customer-engagement/basics/save-advanced-find-search) to search for specific data in the entity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1106">如需在 Common Data Service 中探索個人資料的詳細資料，請參閱[探索 Common Data Service 個人資料](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871881)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1106">For more information around discovering personal data in the Common Data Service, see [Discover Common Data Service personal data](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871881).</span></span>

#### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1107">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1107">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1108">系統管理員可以使用 [PowerApps 系統管理中心](https://admin.powerapps.com/)或 [PowerApps Admin PowerShell Cmdlet](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871804)，將存取和執行應用程式及相關聯資源 (包括流程、連線及自訂連接器) 的權限指派給自己。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1108">Admins have the ability to assign themselves privileges to access and run the apps and associated resources (including flows, connections, and custom connectors) using the [PowerApps Admin Center](https://admin.powerapps.com/) or [PowerApps Admin PowerShell cmdlets](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871804).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p308">在有權存取使用者的應用程式之後，您可以使用網頁瀏覽器來開啟應用程式。在開啟應用程式之後，您可以取得資料的螢幕擷取畫面。請參閱[在網頁瀏覽器中使用 PowerApps](/powerapps/run-app-browser)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p308">After you have access to the user's app, you can use a web browser to open the app. After you open an app, you can take a screenshot of the data. See [Use PowerApps in a web browser](/powerapps/run-app-browser).</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1112">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1112">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1113">因為 PowerApps 可讓使用者組建企業營運應用程式，此應用程式可能是貴組織的關鍵部分，當使用者從貴組織離職且其 Office 365 帳戶遭到刪除時，系統管理員必須決定要刪除使用者所擁有的應用程式，還是只重新指派給新的擁有者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1113">Because PowerApps allow users to build line-of-business application that can be a critical part of your organization's day-to-day operations, when a user leaves your organization and their Office 365 account is deleted, the admin needs to determine whether to delete the apps owned by the user or reassign to new owners.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1114">這是為了協助貴組織將應用程式移轉給新的擁有者，並避免可能用於共用業務流程的應用程式造成業務中斷。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1114">This is to help your organization transition apps to new owners and avoid any disruption to your business for apps that may be used for shared business processes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1115">對於共用資料 (例如應用程式)，系統管理員必須決定要永久刪除該使用者的共用資料，還是將此資料重新指派給自己或其組織內的其他人，來加以保留。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1115">For shared data, like apps, admins must decide whether to permanently delete that user's shared data or keep them by reassigning the data to themselves or someone else within their organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1116">請參閱[刪除 PowerApps 個人資料](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871883)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1116">See [Delete PowerApps personal data](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871883).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p311">使用者儲存在 Common Data Service For Apps 資料庫中實體的任何資料，也會需要由系統管理員檢閱；且必要時，使用產品內功能刪除這些資料。請參閱[刪除 Common Data Service 使用者個人資料](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871886)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p311">Any data that was stored by a user in an entity in a Common Data Service For Apps database will also need to be reviewed and (if desired) deleted by an admin using the in-product capabilities. See [Delete Common Data Service user personal data](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871886).</span></span>

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1119">匯出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1119">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p312">系統管理員可以使用 [PowerApps 系統管理中心](https://admin.powerapps.com/)和 [PowerApps Admin PowerShell Cmdlet](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871804)，針對 PowerApps 服務內的使用者，匯出所儲存的個人資料。請參閱[匯出 PowerApps 個人資料](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871883)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p312">Admins have the ability to export personal data stored for a user within the PowerApps service using the [PowerApps Admin Center](https://admin.powerapps.com/) and [PowerApps Admin PowerShell cmdlets](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871804). See [Export PowerApps personal data](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871883).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p313">您也可以使用[進階尋找](/dynamics365/customer-engagement/basics/save-advanced-find-search)的產品內搜尋功能，搜尋任何實體中的使用者個人資料。如需匯出 Common Data Service 中個人資料的詳細資料，請參閱[匯出 Common Data Service 個人資料](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871889)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p313">You can also use the in-product search capabilities of [Advanced Find](/dynamics365/customer-engagement/basics/save-advanced-find-search) to search for a user's personal data in any entity. For details about exporting personal data in the Common Data Service, see [Export Common Data Service personal data](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871889).</span></span>

#### <a name="connections-and-custom-connectors-in-powerapps"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1124">PowerApps 中的連線和自訂連接器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1124">Connections and custom connectors in PowerApps</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p314">[連線] 需要使用者提供認證，才能連線至 API、SaaS 應用程式，以及自訂開發系統。這些連線是由建立連線的使用者所擁有，並可在產品內[管理](/powerapps/maker/canvas-apps/add-data-connection)。在重新指派 PowerApps 之後，系統管理員可以使用 PowerShell Cmdlet，在刪除使用者資料的過程中列出並刪除這些連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p314">Connections require users to provide credentials to connect to APIs, SaaS applications, and custom developed systems. These connections are owned by the user that established the connection and can be [managed](/powerapps/maker/canvas-apps/add-data-connection) in-product. After PowerApps have been reassigned, an admin can use PowerShell cmdlets to list and delete these connections as part of deleting user data.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p315">自訂連接器可讓組織連線至現成連接器無法使用的系統，來擴充 PowerApps 的功能。自訂連接器作者可將其連接器與組織中的其他人[共用](/connectors/custom-connectors/use-custom-connector-powerapps)。在收到 DSR 刪除要求後，系統管理員應該考慮重新指派這些連接器的擁有權，以避免業務中斷。若要加快此程序，系統管理員可以使用 PowerShell Cmdlet，來列出、重新指派或刪除自訂連接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p315">Custom connectors allow organizations to extend the capabilities of PowerApps by connecting to systems where an out-of-box connector is not available. A custom connector author can [share](/connectors/custom-connectors/use-custom-connector-powerapps) their connector with others in an organization. After receiving a DSR deleting request, an admin should consider reassigning ownership of these connectors to avoid business disruption. To expedite this process, an admin can use PowerShell cmdlets to list, reassign, or delete custom connectors.</span></span>

### <a name="project-online"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1132">Project Online</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1132">Project Online</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1133">下列各節說明如何使用 Microsoft Project Online 中的應用程式內功能，來尋找、存取、匯出及刪除個人資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1133">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Project Online to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover-and-access"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1134">探索和存取</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1134">Discover and access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1135">您可以使用「內容搜尋」來搜尋與 Project 相關聯的 SharePoint Online 網站 (第一次建立 Project 時，會有一個選項用來建立相關聯的 SharePoint Online 網站)；內容搜尋不會搜尋 Project Online 中實際專案內的資料，只會搜尋相關聯的網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1135">You can use Content Search to search the SharePoint Online site that's associated with a Project (when a Project is first created, there's an option to create an associated SharePoint Online site); Content Search doesn't search the data in an actual project in Project Online, only the associated site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1136">雖然「內容搜尋」會搜尋專案的中繼資料，例如主體中提及的人員，不過，這可能有助於您尋找 (和存取) 包含與 DSR 相關資料的專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1136">Though Content Search searches for metadata about projects such as people mentioned in the subject) However, this may help you find (and access) the Project that contains the data related to the DSR.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p317">組織中網站集合的 URL，其中與專案相關聯的網站為 `https://<your org>.sharepoint.com/sites/pwa`；例如，**<https://contoso.sharepoint.com/pwa>**。您可以使用這個特定的網站集合，作為內容搜尋的位置，然後作為搜尋查詢中專案的名稱。此外，IT 系統管理員也可以使用 SharePoint 系統管理中心的 [網站集合] 頁面，取得組織中 PWA 網站集合的清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p317">The URL for the site collection in your organization where sites associated with Projects is `https://<your org>.sharepoint.com/sites/pwa`; for example, **<https://contoso.sharepoint.com/pwa>**. You can use this specific site collection as the location of your content search and then the name of the Project in the search query. Additionally, an IT admin can use the Site Collections page in the SharePoint admin center to get a list of PWA site collections in the organization.</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1140">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1140">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p318">您可以從 Project Online 環境中刪除使用者的相關資訊。請參閱[從 Project Online 中刪除使用者資料](https://support.office.com/article/delete-user-data-from-project-online-252fa593-9c25-47ed-b861-643fe8bf1cb7)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p318">You can delete information about a user from your Project Online environment. See [Delete user data from Project Online](https://support.office.com/article/delete-user-data-from-project-online-252fa593-9c25-47ed-b861-643fe8bf1cb7).</span></span>

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1143">匯出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1143">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p319">您可以從 Project Online 環境中匯出特定使用者的內容。此資料會以 JSON 格式匯出至多個檔案。如需逐步指示，請參閱[從 Project Online 中匯出使用者資料](https://support.office.com/article/export-user-data-from-project-online-27f3838d-3dbe-4b98-80dc-df55f851154d)。如需匯出之檔案的詳細資訊，請參閱 [Project Online 匯出 json 物件定義](https://support.office.com/article/project-online-export-json-object-definitions-ce5faeae-9af4-4696-b847-a1f4f20327c7)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p319">You can a specific user's content from your Project Online environment. This data is exported to multiple files in the JSON format. For step-by instructions see, [Export user data from Project Online](https://support.office.com/article/export-user-data-from-project-online-27f3838d-3dbe-4b98-80dc-df55f851154d). For detailed information about the files that are exported, see [Project Online export json object definitions](https://support.office.com/article/project-online-export-json-object-definitions-ce5faeae-9af4-4696-b847-a1f4f20327c7).</span></span>

### <a name="publisher"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1148">Publisher</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1148">Publisher</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1149">下列各節說明如何使用 Microsoft Publisher 中的應用程式內功能，來尋找、存取、匯出及刪除個人資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1149">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Publisher to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1150">探索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1150">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1151">您可以使用應用程式內的搜尋功能，以您在大部分 Office 應用程式的相同方式，來尋找 Publisher 檔案中的文字。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1151">You can use the in-app search feature to find text in a Publisher file the same way as you can in most Office applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1152">請參閱[尋找及取代文字](https://support.office.com/article/find-and-replace-text-bfe54275-b7c7-4d0f-904d-a2f38d322268)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1152">See [Find and replace text](https://support.office.com/article/find-and-replace-text-bfe54275-b7c7-4d0f-904d-a2f38d322268).</span></span>

#### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1153">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1153">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1154">找到資料之後，就可以取得其螢幕擷取畫面，或複製資料並貼到 Word 或文字檔案，並將該資料提供給資料物件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1154">After you find data, you can take a screenshot of it or copy and paste it into a Word or text file and provide that to the data subject.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1155">您也可以將出版物儲存為 Word、PDF 或 XPS 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1155">You can also save a publication as a Word, PDF, or XPS file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1156">請參閱：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1156">See:</span></span>

  - [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1157">將出版物儲存為 Word 文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1157">Save a publication as a Word document</span></span>](https://support.microsoft.com/office/save-a-publication-as-a-word-document-b5eaaae5-6f1b-48c1-bebc-44460376b693)
  - [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1158">使用 Publisher 將出版物另存新檔為或轉換為 .pdf 或 .xps</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1158">Save As or convert a publication to .pdf or .xps using Publisher</span></span>](https://support.microsoft.com/office/save-as-or-convert-a-publication-to-pdf-or-xps-using-publisher-657332d0-d2c2-464a-9870-e9b3d22e6469)

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1159">匯出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1159">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p322">您可以使用實際 Publisher 檔案提供資料主體，或如先前所述，您可以將出版物另存新檔為 Word、PDF 或 XPS 檔案。請參閲：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p322">You can provide a data subject with the actual Publisher file or as previously explained, you can save a publication as a Word, PDF, or XPS file. See:</span></span>

  - [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1162">將出版物儲存為 Word 文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1162">Save a publication as a Word document</span></span>](https://support.microsoft.com/office/save-a-publication-as-a-word-document-b5eaaae5-6f1b-48c1-bebc-44460376b693)

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1164">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1164">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1165">您可以刪除出版物中的內容、刪除整個頁面，或刪除整個 Publisher 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1165">You can delete content from a publication, delete entire pages, or delete an entire Publisher file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1166">請參閱[新增或刪除頁面](https://support.office.com/article/add-or-delete-pages-daf71e39-86e0-4bbc-a186-d5ec70450b08)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1166">See [Add or delete pages](https://support.office.com/article/add-or-delete-pages-daf71e39-86e0-4bbc-a186-d5ec70450b08).</span></span>

### <a name="stream"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1167">Stream</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1167">Stream</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1168">下列各節說明如何使用 Microsoft Stream 中的應用程式內功能，來尋找、存取、匯出及刪除個人資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1168">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Stream to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1169">探索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1169">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p324">若要探索已產生或上傳至 Stream 並可能與資料主體要求相關的內容，Stream 系統管理員可以執行使用者報告，判斷 Stream 使用者可能已上傳、建立或張貼哪些影片、影片描述、群組、頻道或評論。如需如何產生報告的指示，請參閱[在 Microsoft Stream 中管理使用者資料](/stream/managing-user-data)。報告輸出為 HTML 格式，包含可用來瀏覽到可能感興趣影片的超連結。如果您想要檢視設定自訂權限的影片，而您不屬於影片訴求對象的原始使用者，您可以用系統管理模式檢視，請參閱 [Microsoft Stream 中的系統管理員功能](/stream/manage-content-permissions)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p324">To discover content that is generated or uploaded to Stream that may be relevant to a data subject request, a Stream admin can run a user report to determine what videos, video descriptions, groups, channels, or comments a Stream user may have uploaded, created, or posted by a user. For instructions on how to generate a report, see [Managing user data in Microsoft Stream](/stream/managing-user-data). The report output is in HTML format and contains hyperlinks that can be used to navigate to videos of potential interest. If you would like to view a video that has custom permission set and you are not part of the original users for whom the video was intended, you can view in admin mode, See [Admin capabilities in Microsoft Stream](/stream/manage-content-permissions).</span></span>  

#### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1174">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1174">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p325">根據資料主體要求的本質，上述的報告有助於滿足資料主體要求。使用者報告包括 Stream 使用者的名稱和唯一識別碼、使用者上傳的影片清單、使用者可存取的影片清單、使用者建立的頻道清單、使用者所屬的所有群組清單，以及使用者對影片留下的所有評論清單。這份報告更進一步顯示該使用者是否已檢視使用者報告中所列的每部影片。如果您想要將影片存取權提供給資料主體以滿足 DSR 要求，您可以共用該影片。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p325">Depending on the nature of the data subject request, a copy of the report described above can be used help satisfy a data subject request. The user report includes the Stream user's name and unique ID, a list of videos the user uploaded, a list of videos the user has access to, a list of channels the user created, a list of all the groups the user is a member of, and a list of all comments the user left on videos. The report further shows whether the user viewed each video listed in the user report. If you would like to provide the data subject with access to a video to satisfy a DSR request, you can share the video.</span></span>

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1179">匯出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1179">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1180">請參閱 Stream 的「存取」一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1180">See the Access section for Stream.</span></span> 

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1181">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1181">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p326">若要刪除或編輯影片或任何其他 Stream 內容，Stream 系統管理員可以選取用系統管理模式檢視，以執行所需的功能。請參閱 [Microsoft Stream 中的系統管理員功能](/stream/manage-content-permissions)。如果使用者已離開組織，而且希望移除其名稱，使其不要出現在其上傳影片的旁邊，您可以移除他們的名稱或以另一個名稱取代之。請參閱[在 Microsoft Stream 中管理已刪除的使用者](/stream/managing-deleted-users)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p326">To delete or edit videos or any other Stream content, a Stream admin can select view in admin mode to perform the necessary function. See [Admin capabilities in Microsoft Stream](/stream/manage-content-permissions). If a user has left the organization and would like to have their name removed from appearing next to videos that they uploaded, you can remove their name or replace it with another. See [Managing deleted users in Microsoft Stream](/stream/managing-deleted-users).</span></span>

### <a name="sway"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1186">Sway</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1186">Sway</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1187">下列各節說明如何使用 Microsoft Sway 中的應用程式內功能，來尋找、存取、匯出及刪除個人資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1187">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Sway to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1188">探索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1188">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1189">只有擁有者和經過作者允許的人員，才能檢視使用 Sway 所建立的內容 (可在 [www.sway.com](https://sway.office.com/) 找到)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1189">Content created using Sway (found at [www.sway.com](https://sway.office.com/)) can only be seen by the owner and those that the author has permitted to view the Sway.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1190">請參閱 [Sway 的隱私權設定](https://support.microsoft.com/office/privacy-settings-in-sway-394b551c-be6f-4bd7-a70a-f318d72bf217)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1190">See [Privacy Settings in Sway](https://support.microsoft.com/office/privacy-settings-in-sway-394b551c-be6f-4bd7-a70a-f318d72bf217).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1191">若要判斷 Sway 是否為可回應 DSR 的個人資料可能存在的位置，您可以要求資料主體和可能產生資料主題相關內容的組織使用者搜尋其 Sway，並與您共用可能包含可回應資料主體要求之個人資料的任何 Sway。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1191">To determine whether Sway is a place where personal data responsive to your DSR is likely to reside, you can ask the Data Subject and organizational users who are likely to have generated content about the Data Subject to search their Sways and share with you any Sways that are likely to contain personal data responsive to the Data Subject's request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1192">如需如何共用 Sway 的相關資訊，請參閱[共用您的 Sway](https://support.microsoft.com/office/share-your-sway-1cf853b8-ef7e-46b0-b704-003e58d28998) 一文中的＜從您的組織帳戶共用 Sway＞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1192">For information on how to share a Sway, see "Share a Sway from your Organizational Account" in this [Share your Sway](https://support.microsoft.com/office/share-your-sway-1cf853b8-ef7e-46b0-b704-003e58d28998) article.</span></span>

#### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1193">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1193">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p328">如果您在 Sway 中找到想要與資料主體共用的個人資料，可讓資料主體透過下列幾種方式之一存取資料。您可以將 Sway 線上版本的複本提供給資料主體 (如上述)；也可以針對 Sway 中想共用的相關部分，取得幕擷取畫面；或者將 Sway 列印出來、下載至 Word 中，或將其轉換為 PDF 檔案。下方的「匯出」章節會進一步說明如何下載 Sway。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p328">If you have found personal data in a Sway that you would like to share with the Data Subject, you can provide the Data Subject with access to the data through one of several means. You can provide the Data Subject a copy of the online version of Sway (as described above); you can take screenshots of the relevant portion of the Sway that you would like to share; or you can print or download the Sway to Word or convert it to a PDF. How to download a Sway is further described in the "export" section below.</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1197">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1197">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p329">若要了解如何刪除 Sway，請移至 [Sway 的隱私權設定](https://support.microsoft.com/office/privacy-settings-in-sway-394b551c-be6f-4bd7-a70a-f318d72bf217)中的＜如何刪除我的 Sway？＞一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p329">To learn how to delete a Sway, go to the "How do I delete my Sway?" section in [Privacy settings in Sway](https://support.microsoft.com/office/privacy-settings-in-sway-394b551c-be6f-4bd7-a70a-f318d72bf217).</span></span>

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1200">匯出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1200">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1201">若要匯出 Sway，請開啟您想要下載的 Sway、在左上角選取一連串的點 (省略符號)、選取 [匯出]，然後選擇 [Word] 或 [PDF]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1201">To export a Sway, open the Sway that you would like to download, select the series of dots (ellipsis) in the upper right corner, select **Export,** and then choose either **Word** or **PDF**.</span></span>

### <a name="whiteboard"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1202">Whiteboard</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1202">Whiteboard</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1203">下列各節說明如何使用 Microsoft Whiteboard 中的應用程式內功能，來尋找、存取、匯出及刪除個人資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1203">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Whiteboard to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1204">Surface Hub 上的 Whiteboard 2016</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1204">Whiteboard 2016 on Surface Hub</span></span>](#whiteboard-2016-on-surface-hub)
- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1205">其他所有平台上的 Whiteboard</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1205">Whiteboard on all other platforms</span></span>](#whiteboard-for-pc-surface-hub-and-other-platforms)

#### <a name="whiteboard-2016-on-surface-hub"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1206">Surface Hub 上的 Whiteboard 2016</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1206">Whiteboard 2016 on Surface Hub</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1207">本節說明如何針對在 Surface Hub 上使用內建 Whiteboard 2016 應用程式建立的資料來回應 DSR 要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1207">This section describes responding to DSR requests for data created using the built-in Whiteboard 2016 app on Surface Hub.</span></span>

##### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1208">探索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1208">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p330">Whiteboard 檔案 (.wbx 檔案) 會儲存在使用者的商務用 OneDrive 帳戶中。如果他們建立的白板可能包含可回應 DSR 要求的個人資料，您可以詢問資料主體或其他使用者。他們可以與您共用白板，您也可以取得其複本來提供給資料主體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p330">Whiteboard files (.wbx files) are stored in users' OneDrive for Business account. You can ask the data subject or other users if whiteboards they created may contain personal data responsive to a DSR request. They can share a whiteboard with you, or you can get a copy of it to give to the data subject.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1212">若要存取及移轉白板：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1212">To access and transfer whiteboards:</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p331">授與您自己存取使用者之商務用 OneDrive 帳戶的權限。請參閱[存取及備份先前使用者的資料](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/get-access-to-and-back-up-a-former-user-s-data)中的＜存取離職員工的商務用 OneDrive 文件＞一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p331">Give yourself access to the user's OneDrive for Business account.
