See the "Get access to the former employee's OneDrive for Business documents" section in [Get access to and back up a former user's data](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/get-access-to-and-back-up-a-former-user-s-data).</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1215">移至使用者的商務用 OneDrive 帳戶中的 [Whiteboard 應用程式資料] 資料夾，並且複製您要移轉之白板的 .wbx 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1215">Go to the Whiteboard App Data folder in the user's OneDrive for Business account and copy the .wbx files of the whiteboards that you want to transfer.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1216">授與您自己存取資料主體之商務用 OneDrive 帳戶的權限，然後移至 [Whiteboard 應用程式資料] 資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1216">Give yourself access to the data subject's OneDrive for Business account, and then go to Whiteboard App Data folder.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1217">貼上您在上一步中複製的 .wbx 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1217">Paste the .wbx files that you copied in the previous step.</span></span>

##### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1218">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1218">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1219">如果您在可回應 DSR 存取要求的白板中尋找個人資料，您可以用下列幾種方式提供白板的資料主體存取權：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1219">If you find personal data in a whiteboard that's responsive to a DSR access request, you can provide the data subject access to a whiteboard in several ways:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1220">取得白板相關部分的螢幕擷取畫面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1220">Take screenshots of the relevant portions of a whiteboard.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p332">將 .wbx 檔案的複本上傳到資料主體的商務用 OneDrive 帳戶。請參閱前一節中存取及移轉 .wbx 檔案的步驟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p332">Upload a copy of the .wbx file to the data subject's OneDrive for Business account. See the previous section for steps on accessing and transferring .wbx files.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1223">將白板複本儲存為 .png 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1223">Export a copy of whiteboard as a .png file.</span></span>

##### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1224">匯出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1224">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1225">如果您已取得白板的複本，即可將它匯出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1225">If you've obtained a copy of a whiteboard, you can export it.</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1226">在 Surface Hub 上啟動 Whiteboard。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1226">Launch Whiteboard on the Surface Hub.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p333">點選 [共用] 按鈕，然後選取 [匯出複本]。您可以將白板匯出為 OneNote (.one) 檔案或影像 (.png) 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p333">Tap the Share button and then select Export a copy. You can export a whiteboard to a OneNote (.one) file or to an image (.png) file.</span></span>

##### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1229">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1229">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1230">您可以授與自己存取使用者之商務用 OneDrive 帳戶的權限，然後刪除白板。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1230">You can give yourself access to the user's OneDrive for Business account and then delete the whiteboards.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p334">授與您自己存取資料主體之商務用 OneDrive 帳戶的權限。請參閱[存取及備份先前使用者的資料](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/get-access-to-and-back-up-a-former-user-s-data)中的＜存取離職員工的商務用 OneDrive 文件＞一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p334">Give yourself access to the data subject's OneDrive for Business account. See the "Get access to the former employee's OneDrive for Business documents" section in [Get access to and back up a former user's data](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/get-access-to-and-back-up-a-former-user-s-data)</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1233">移至 [Whiteboard 應用程式資料] 資料夾，然後刪除此資料夾的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1233">Go to the Whiteboard App Data folder and then delete the contents of this folder.</span></span>

#### <a name="whiteboard-for-pc-surface-hub-and-other-platforms"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1234">適用於電腦、Surface Hub 及其他平台的 Whiteboard</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1234">Whiteboard for PC, Surface Hub, and other platforms</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p335">如果系統管理員在新 Whiteboard 應用程式中收到對於資料的 DSR 要求，他們可以使用 Whiteboard PowerShell 將自己 (或其他使用者) 新增為使用者白板的擁有者。這可讓系統管理員執行動作，包括存取、匯出及刪除白板。使用 **Set-WhiteboardOwner** Cmdlet，將您自己或其他使用者新增為白板的擁有者，或使用 **Invoke-TransferAllWhiteboards** Cmdlet 將特定使用者的所有白板擁有權移轉給新的擁有者。如需有關使用這些 Cmdlet 及安裝 Whiteboard PowerShell 模組的相關資訊，請參閱 Microsoft Whiteboard Cmdlet 參考。在您或其他人員具有白板的擁有權之後，請參閱 [Microsoft Whiteboard Cmdlet 參考](/powershell/module/whiteboard/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p335">If an admin receives a DSR request for data in the new Whiteboard app, they can use Whiteboard PowerShell to add themselves (or other users) as an owner of a user's whiteboards. This enables an admin to perform actions including accessing, exporting, and deleting whiteboards. Use either the **Set-WhiteboardOwner** cmdlet to add yourself or another user as the owner of a whiteboard or use the **Invoke-TransferAllWhiteboards** cmdlet to transfer the ownership of all whiteboards for a specific user to a new owner. For information about using these cmdlets and installing the Whiteboard PowerShell module, see Microsoft Whiteboard cmdlet reference. After you or another person has ownership of a whiteboard, see [Microsoft Whiteboard cmdlet reference](/powershell/module/whiteboard/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1240">在您或其他人員具有白板的擁有權之後，如需存取、匯出及刪除白板的詳細指引，請參閱 [Microsoft 白板說明](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=872780)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1240">After you or another person has ownership of a whiteboard, see the [Whiteboard support article](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=872780) for detailed guidance about accessing, exporting, and deleting whiteboards.</span></span>

### <a name="yammer"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1241">Yammer</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1241">Yammer</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1242">下列各節說明如何使用 Microsoft Yammer 中的應用程式內功能，來尋找、存取、匯出及刪除個人資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1242">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Yammer to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1243">探索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1243">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1244">從 Yammer 系統管理中心，Yammer 驗證管理員 (全域系統管理員或在 Yammer 中設定的驗證管理員) 可以匯出與特定使用者相關的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1244">From the Yammer admin center, a Yammer verified admin (global admin or verified admin set up in Yammer) can export data pertaining to a given user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1245">匯出包含使用者所張貼及修改的訊息和檔案，以及使用者所建立的主題和群組的相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1245">The export includes the messages and files posted and modified by the user, and information about topics and groups created by the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1246">執行使用者特定資料匯出時，系統管理員也會收到收件匣訊息，其中附有使用者的帳戶活動資料；若系統管理員有意願，可將此資枓提供給使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1246">When a user-specific data export is run, the admin will also receive an inbox message with the user's account activity data that they can provide to the user if they so choose.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1247">如需詳細指示，請參閱 [Yammer Enterprise：隱私權](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1247">For detailed instructions, see [Yammer Enterprise: Privacy](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1248">使用者特定匯出適用於單一網路；因此若使用者位於外部 Yammer 網路，則系統管理員必須針對該外部網路，以及針對家用網路匯出資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1248">User-specific exports are for a single network, so if the user is in an external Yammer network, the admin must export data for that external network, and for the home network.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1249">若要存取資料匯出中未包含的資料，可以針對使用者設定檔、設定、群組成員資格、加上書籤的訊息、追蹤的使用者以及追蹤的主題，取得螢幕擷取畫面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1249">To access data not included in data export, screenshots can be taken for the user's profile, settings, group memberships, bookmarked messages, followed users, and followed topics.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1250">使用者或系統管理員可以收集這些資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1250">Users or admins can collect this information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1251">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [Yammer Enterprise：隱私權](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1251">For more information, see [Yammer Enterprise: Privacy](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise).</span></span>

#### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1252">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1252">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p338">您可以檢視所匯出檔案中的資料，包括訊息的全文和檔案的內容。您也可以按一下所匯出檔案中的連結，直接移至 Yammer 中張貼的訊息和檔案，以及移至群組、使用者建立的主題、使用者喜歡的訊息、使用者為 @mentioned 的訊息、使用者已投票的民意調查和使用者已新增的連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p338">You can view data in the exported files, including the full text of messages and the contents of files. You can also select links in the exported files to go directly to the posted messages and files in Yammer, and to groups, and topics the user created, messages the user liked, messages where the user is @mentioned, polls the user has voted on, and links the user has added.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1255">每一使用者的資料匯出不包括：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1255">Per-user data export does not include:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1256">使用者的設定檔：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1256">The user's profile:</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p339">如果使用者具有 Yammer 身分識別，使用者可以完全控制其設定檔。如需怎樣檢視和修改設定檔的相關資訊，請參閱[變更我的 Yammer 設定檔和設定](https://support.office.com/article/change-my-yammer-profile-and-settings-a3aeca0e-de34-4897-9b59-de6516542851)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p339">If the user has a Yammer identity, the user has full control of their profile. For information on how to view and modify the profile, see [Change my Yammer profile and settings](https://support.office.com/article/change-my-yammer-profile-and-settings-a3aeca0e-de34-4897-9b59-de6516542851).</span></span>
    
    - <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p340">如果使用者具有 Office 365 身分識別，系統會自動從 Office 365 帶入 Yammer 使用者設定檔；這會從 Azure Active Directory (AAD) 取得設定檔資訊。Yammer 使用者可以暫時變更自己在 Yammer 的設定檔；但在 AAD 中發生變更時，會覆寫前者，因此您必須檢視並變更 AAD 中的目錄資料。請參閱[從 Office 365 跨其生命週期管理 Yammer 使用者](/yammer/manage-yammer-users/manage-users-across-their-lifecycle)和[新增或變更 Azure Active Directory 中使用者的設定檔資訊](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-users-profile-azure-portal)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p340">If the user has an Office 365 identity, the Yammer user profile is pulled automatically from Office 365, which gets the profile information from Azure Active Directory (AAD). Yammer users can temporarily change their profiles in Yammer, but these changes are overwritten when there is a change in AAD, so you must view and change directory data in AAD. See [Manage Yammer users across their lifecycle from Office 365](/yammer/manage-yammer-users/manage-users-across-their-lifecycle) and [Add or change profile information for a user in Azure Active Directory](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-users-profile-azure-portal).</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1262">使用者的設定：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1262">The user's settings:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1263">使用者可以檢視和變更自己的設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1263">The user can view and change their own settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1264">如需如何檢視和修改使用者設定的相關資訊，請參閱[變更我的 Yammer 設定檔和設定](https://support.office.com/article/change-my-yammer-profile-and-settings-a3aeca0e-de34-4897-9b59-de6516542851)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1264">For information on how to view and modify user settings, see [Change my Yammer profile and settings](https://support.office.com/article/change-my-yammer-profile-and-settings-a3aeca0e-de34-4897-9b59-de6516542851).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1265">系統管理員可以檢視此資訊並取得螢幕擷取畫面，但無法變更該資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1265">An admin can view this information and take screenshots, but can't change it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1266">移至 Yammer 設定 \> [人員 **]**，然後選取使用者的名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1266">Go to Yammer settings \> **People**, and then select the name of the user.</span></span><br/>
    - <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1267">使用者的群組成員資格、加上書籤的訊息、追蹤的使用者，以及追蹤的主題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1267">The user's group membership, bookmarked messages, followed users, and followed topics.</span></span>
    
    - <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1268">使用者可以檢視此資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1268">The user can view this information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1269">如需做法的相關資訊，請參閱[在 Yammer 保持井然有序的提示](https://support.office.com/article/tips-for-staying-organized-in-yammer-40ae9666-75c0-4254-a84c-d87a9542f380)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1269">For information on how, see [Tips for staying organized in Yammer](https://support.office.com/article/tips-for-staying-organized-in-yammer-40ae9666-75c0-4254-a84c-d87a9542f380).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1270">系統管理員可以檢視此資訊並取得螢幕擷取畫面，但無法變更該資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1270">An admin can view this information and take screenshots, but can't change it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1271">移至 Yammer 設定 \> [人員 **]**，然後選取使用者的名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1271">Go to Yammer settings \> **People**, and then select the name of the user.</span></span>

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1272">匯出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1272">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p343">如需怎樣匯出資料的指示，請參閱[管理 Yammer Enterprise 中的 GDPR 資料主體要求](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise)。您必須針對使用者為其成員的每個 Yammer 網路，執行按使用者匯出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p343">For instructions for how to export data, see [Manage GDPR data subject requests in Yammer Enterprise](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise). You must run a per-user export for each Yammer network the user is a member of.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p344">Yammer 具有資料保留設定；當使用者刪除訊息或檔案時，這些設定會虛刪除或實刪除資料。若將其設為虛刪除，則使用者已刪除的資料將會包含在匯出內。如果 Yammer 資料保留設定設為實刪除，則已刪除的資訊不會再儲存在 Yammer 中，因此不會包含在匯出內。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p344">Yammer has data retention settings that either soft-delete or hard-delete data when a user deletes a message or file. If this is set to soft-delete, data a user has deleted will be included in the export. If the Yammer data retention setting is set to hard-delete, the deleted information is no longer stored in Yammer, so will not be included in the export.</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1278">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1278">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p345">如果驗證管理員收到 DSR，Yammer 可讓驗證管理員透過 Yammer 系統管理中心，執行符合 GDPR 規範的刪除。此選項稱為 [清除使用者]，會將使用者暫停 14 天，然後移除其所有個人資料，但檔案和訊息除外。如果使用者是來賓使用者，則必須針對來賓是其成員的每個外部網路執行此動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p345">Yammer allows verified admins to execute a GDPR-compliant delete via the Yammer admin center if they receive a DSR. This option is called Erase User, and it suspends the user for 14 days and then removes all their personal data, excluding files and messages. If the user is a guest user, this must be done for each external network the guest is a member of.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p346">如果系統管理員想要在 14 天的時間範圍內移除使用者的檔案和訊息，則他們必須執行使用者層級匯出，來識別檔案和訊息，然後決定要透過產品內刪除，或使用 PowerShell 指令碼刪除哪些檔案和訊息。在 14 天的時間範圍後，系統管理員就無法再讓使用者與其檔案或訊息產生關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p346">If an admin wants to remove the files and messages of a user during the 14-day window, they will have to perform a user level export to identify the files and messages, and then decide which ones to delete either by in-product deletion or by using a PowerShell script. After the 14-day window, the admin can no longer associate the user with their files or messages.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p347">使用 [清除使用者] 選項來刪除使用者時，系統會將通知傳送至所有網路管理員和驗證管理員的 Yammer 收件匣。[清除使用者] 選項會清除使用者的 Yammer 設定檔案，但不會刪除其 Office 365 或 Azure Active Directory 設定檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p347">When a user is deleted with the Erase User option, notification is sent to the Yammer Inbox of all network admins and verified admins. The Erase User option deletes the user's Yammer profile, but does not delete their Office 365 or Azure Active Directory profile.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1286">如需移除使用者的詳細步驟，請參閱[管理 Yammer Enterprise 中的 GDPR 資料主體要求](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1286">For detailed steps to remove a user, see [Manage GDPR data subject requests in Yammer Enterprise](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise).</span></span>

## <a name="responding-to-dsr-rectification-requests"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1287">回應 DSR 修正要求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1287">Responding to DSR rectification requests</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p348">如果資料主體要求您修正個人資料，而此個人資料常駐在 Office 365 中儲存的貴組織資料內，則您和貴組織必須判斷接受要求是否適當。如果您選擇接受要求，修正資料可能包含採取下列動作，例如：從文件或其他類型的項目中，編輯、刪減或移除個人資料。最方便的方式是要求資料/文件擁有者，使用適當的 Office 365 應用程式來進行所要求的變更。替代方法為讓貴組織中的 IT 系統管理員進行變更。這可能需要 IT 系統管理員 (或貴組織中具有適當權限的其他人員，例如 SharePoint Online 網站集合管理員) 將存取文件或文件所在內容位置的必要權限，指派給自己或處理 DSR 的其他人，以便直接對文件進行變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p348">If a data subject has asked you to rectify the personal data that resides in your organization's data stored in Office 365, you and your organization have to determine whether it's appropriate to honor the request. If you choose to honor the request, then rectifying the data may include taking actions such as editing, redacting, or removing personal data from a document or other type or item. The most expedient way to do this is to ask the data/document owner to use the appropriate Office 365 application to make the requested change. An alternative is to have an IT admin in your organization make the change. This will probably require the IT admin (or other people in your organization with the appropriate privileges, such as a SharePoint Online site collection administrator) to assign to themselves or someone else working on the DSR the necessary permissions to gain access to the document or the content location where the document is located to make the change directly to the document.</span></span>

### <a name="requesting-that-the-data-owner-to-make-the-approved-change"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1293">要求資料擁有者進行經核准的變更</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1293">Requesting that the data owner to make the approved change</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p349">修正個人資料最直接的方式，就是要求資料擁有者進行變更。在找出作為 DSR 主體的資料之後，您可以提供下列資訊，讓資料擁有者能進行變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p349">The most direct way to rectify personal data is to ask the data owner to make the change. After you locate the data that is the subject of the DSR, you can provide the following information so that they can make the change.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p350">需要變更之項目的位置和檔案名稱 (適用於文件和其他檔案)；定位有問題的資料是先前說明的探索程序[探索程序](#using-content-search-to-find-personal-data)的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p350">The location and file name (for documents and other files) of the item that needs to be changed. Locating the data in question is part of the discovery process [discovery process](#using-content-search-to-find-personal-data) that was previously explained.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1298">資料擁有者應該進行的經核准變更</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1298">The approved change the data owner should make</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1299">建議您考慮實施確認程序，讓您或參與 DSR 調查的其他人確認是否已進行所要求的變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1299">You may want to consider implementing a confirmation process where you or another person involved in the DSR investigation verifies that the requested change has been made.</span></span>

### <a name="gaining-access-to-a-sharepoint-online-site-or-onedrive-for-business-account-to-make-changes"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1300">存取 SharePoint Online 網站或商務用 OneDrive 帳戶進行變更</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1300">Gaining access to a SharePoint Online site or OneDrive for Business account to make changes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p351">若無法讓資料擁有者實作資料主體的修正要求，則貴組織中的 IT 系統管理員或 SharePoint Online 系統管理員可以存取內容位置，並進行所需的變更。或者，系統管理員也可將必要的權限指派給您或其他資料隱私權主管。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p351">If it's not feasible for the data owner to implement the data subject's request for rectification, an IT admin or SharePoint admin in your organization can get access to the content location and make the required changes. Or, an admin can assign you or another data privacy officer the necessary permissions.</span></span>

#### <a name="sharepoint-online"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1303">SharePoint Online</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1303">SharePoint Online</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1304">若要指派 Sharepoint 網站的系統管理員或擁有者權限，以便您或其他人可以存取及編輯該文件，請參閱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1304">To assign administrator or owner permissions to a SharePoint Online site so that you or someone else can access and edit that document, see</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1305">管理網站集合的系統管理員</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1305">Manage administrators for a site collection</span></span>](/sharepoint/manage-site-collection-administrators)

- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1306">編輯和管理 SharePoint 清單或文件庫的權限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1306">Edit and manage permissions for a SharePoint list or library</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/Edit-and-manage-permissions-for-a-SharePoint-list-or-library-02d770f3-59eb-4910-a608-5f84cc297782)

#### <a name="onedrive-for-business"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1307">商務用 OneDrive</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1307">OneDrive for Business</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1308">全域系統管理員可以存取使用者的商務用 OneDrive 帳戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1308">A global admin can access a user's OneDrive for Business account by using the .</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1309">使用全域系統管理員認證登入 Office 365。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1309">Sign in to Office 365 with your global admin credentials.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1310">移至系統管理中心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1310">Go to the admin center.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1311">移至 [作用中使用者 **]**，然後選取使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1311">Go to **Active users** and select the user.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1312">展開詳細資料窗格中的 [商務用 OneDrive 設定 **]**，然後選取 [存取檔案 **]**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1312">Expand **OneDrive for Business Settings** in the details pane, and then select **Access files**.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1313">選取 URL 來移至使用者的商務用 OneDrive 帳戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1313">select the URL to go to the user's OneDrive for Business account.</span></span>

### <a name="gaining-access-to-an-exchange-online-mailbox-to-make-changes-to-data"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1314">取得 Exchange Online 信箱的存取權，以對資料進行變更</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1314">Gaining access to an Exchange Online mailbox to make changes to data</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p352">全域系統管理員可將開啟和編輯 (或刪除) 其他使用者信箱中的項目 (就好像自己是信箱擁有者一樣) 所需的權利指派給自己。全域系統管理員也可以將這些權限指派給另一位使用者。具體來說，全域系統管理員需要新增 **讀取及管理** 權限，即 Exchange Online 中的完整存取權利。如需詳細資料，請參閱：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p352">A global admin can assign themselves the permissions necessary to open and edit (or delete) items in another user's mailbox, as if they were the mailbox owner. A global admin can also assign these permissions to another user. Specifically, the global admin needs to add the **Read and manage** permission, which is the Full Access permission in Exchange Online. For details, see:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1319">將信箱權限授與 Office 365 中的其他使用者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1319">Give mailbox permissions to another user in Office 365</span></span>](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/give-mailbox-permissions-to-another-user)
- [<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1320">存取另一個人員的信箱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1320">Access another person's mailbox</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/Access-another-person-s-mailbox-A909AD30-E413-40B5-A487-0EA70B763081)

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p353">如果使用者信箱設有法務保存措施，或已指派給保留原則，則會保留信箱的所有版本，直到保留期間到期，或從信箱中移除保留。這表示，如果變更信箱項目以回應 DSR 修正要求，則會保留原始項目的複本 (在進行變更之前)，並儲存在使用者信箱的 [可復原項目] 資料夾中的隱藏資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p353">If the user mailbox is place on a legal hold or has been assigned to a retention policy, all versions of a mailbox are retained until the retention period expires or the hold is removed from the mailbox. That means if a mailbox item is changed in response to DSR rectification request, a copy of original item (before the change was made) is retained and stored in a hidden folder in the Recoverable Items folder in the user's mailbox.</span></span>

### <a name="making-changes-to-content-in-onedrive-for-business-and-sharepoint-online"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1323">對商務用 OneDrive 和 SharePoint Online 中的內容進行變更</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1323">Making changes to content in OneDrive for Business and SharePoint Online</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p354">系統管理員或資料擁有者可對 SharePoint Online 文件、清單和頁面進行變更。在對 SharePoint 內容進行變更時，請記住下列事項：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p354">Admins or data owners can make changes to SharePoint Online documents, lists, and pages. Keep the following things in mind when making changes to SharePoint content:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1326">更新文件將儲存文件的新版本，其中將包含修訂。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1326">Updating a document saves a new version of the document, which will contain the revision.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1327">較舊版本的文件將不會更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1327">Older versions of the document will not be updated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1328">這表示，作為 DSR 修正要求主體的資料，可能會持續保存在較舊版本的主題中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1328">That means it's possible that the data that's the subject of a DSR rectification request may persist in older versions of the topic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1329">您可以刪除較舊版本的主題，然後從 Office 365 中永久移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1329">Older versions of a topic can be deleted and then permanently removed from Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1330">請參閱本指南中的[刪除 SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 中的文件](#deleting-documents-in-sharepoint-online-and-onedrive-for-business)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1330">See the [Deleting documents in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business](#deleting-documents-in-sharepoint-online-and-onedrive-for-business) section in this guide.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1331">若要以從檔案中移除資料主體之所有追蹤的方式來刪減 SharePoint 檔案，包括所有版本的檔案和資料主體所執行的所有記錄活動，您必須執行下列步驟：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1331">To completely redact a SharePoint file in a way that removes all traces of a data subject from the file, including all versions of the file and all recorded activity performed by the data subject, you have to perform the following steps:</span></span>

    1. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1332">將檔案的複本下載到本機電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1332">Download a copy of the file to your local computer.</span></span>
    2. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p356">請從 SharePoint Online 中先刪除檔案，然後從第一階段和第二階段資源回收筒刪除，以便永久刪除檔案。請參閱本指南中的[刪除 SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 中的文件](#deleting-documents-in-sharepoint-online-and-onedrive-for-business)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p356">Permanently delete the file from SharePoint Online, by deleting the file, and then deleting if from the first-stage and second-stage Recycle Bin. See the [Deleting documents in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business](#deleting-documents-in-sharepoint-online-and-onedrive-for-business) section in this guide.</span></span>
    3. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1335">對本機電腦上的文件複本進行修訂。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1335">Make the revisions to the copy of the document on your local computer.</span></span>
    4. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1336">將修訂後的檔案上傳至原始 SharePoint Online 位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1336">Upload the revised file to the original SharePoint Online location.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p357">可以編輯 SharePoint 清單中的資料。請參閱[新增、編輯或刪除清單項目](https://support.microsoft.com/office/add-edit-or-delete-list-items-a4b31f53-f044-470e-9823-4526594bacde)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p357">Data in SharePoint lists can be edited. See [Add, edit, or delete list items](https://support.microsoft.com/office/add-edit-or-delete-list-items-a4b31f53-f044-470e-9823-4526594bacde).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1339">IT 系統管理員也可以更正與文件相關聯的特定個人內容：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1339">IT admins can also correct certain personal properties associated with a document:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p358">來自 SharePoint 使用者設定檔或 Office 365 的使用者資訊通常與商務用 OneDrive 和 SharePoint Online 文件相關聯，以代表該人員。例如，文件或清單項目的 [建立者] 或 [修改者] 欄位中的使用者名稱。有數種方式可修正此使用者資訊，視來源而定：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p358">User information from the SharePoint User Profile or Office 365 is often associated with OneDrive for Business and SharePoint Online documents to represent that person. For example, a user's name in a Created By or Modified By People column for a document or list item. This user information can be rectified in several ways, depending on the source:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p359">修正自己內部部署的 Active Directory 中的使用者內容。對於會同步處理使用者屬性 (例如來自內部部署 AD 的使用者顯示名稱、名字等) 的客戶，應該在內部部署的 Active Directory 中修正這些內容。適當對應的內容會流入 Office 365，再流入商務用 OneDrive 和 SharePoint Online。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p359">Rectify user properties in their own on-premises Active Directory. For customers syncing user properties such as user Display Name, First Name, etc. from an on-premises AD, those properties should be rectified there. Appropriately mapped properties flow into Office 365, and then OneDrive for Business and SharePoint Online.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1346">修正系統管理中心的使用者內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1346">Rectify user properties in the admin center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1347">在這裡對帳戶資訊所做的變更會自動反映在商務用 OneDrive 和 SharePoint Online 體驗中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1347">Changes made to account information there will automatically be reflected in OneDrive for Business and SharePoint Online experiences.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1348">如需資訊，請參閱[新增或變更 Azure Active Directory 中使用者的設定檔資訊](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=864809)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1348">For info, see [Add or change profile information for a user in Azure Active Directory](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=864809).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1349">對於來源為 Office 365 的內容，您無法從 SharePoint 端進行任何變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1349">For properties sourced in Office 365, no changes can be made on the SharePoint side.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1350">修正 SharePoint 系統管理中心的 SharePoint 使用者設定檔體驗中的使用者內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1350">Rectify user properties in the SharePoint user profile experience of the SharePoint admin center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1351">在 SharePoint 系統管理中心的 [使用者設定檔] 索引標籤中，系統管理員可以選取 [管理使用者設定檔 **]**，並查看任何使用者的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1351">In the user profiles tab of the SharePoint admin center, admins can select **Manage user profiles**, and look up any user's properties.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1352">然後，他們就可以選擇編輯使用者的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1352">Then they can choose to Edit the user's properties.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p362">修正自訂來源中的使用者內容。自訂 SharePoint 設定檔內容可以透過 Microsoft Identity Manager (MIM) 或另一種方法，從自訂來源進行同步處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p362">Rectify user properties in a custom source. Custom SharePoint profile properties may be syncing from a custom source via Microsoft Identity Manager (MIM) or another method.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p363">這不會影響所有體驗，但可能會保留較舊的資訊。例如，文件中以文字表示的使用者名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p363">This won't affect all experiences, which may retain the older information. For example, the user's name as text in the document.</span></span>

### <a name="making-changes-to-content-in-power-bi"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1357">對 Power BI 中的內容進行變更</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1357">Making changes to content in Power BI</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p364">Power BI 依賴用於其儀表板和報告的基礎來源資料，才能完整且精確，所以必須在基礎來源資料中更正不精確或不完整的來源資料。例如，如果您建立了連線至 Dynamics 365 for Sales 的 Power BI 報告，作為即時資料來源，則您必須在 Dynamics 365 for Sales 中對資料進行所有更正。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p364">Power BI relies on the underlying source data used in its dashboards and reports to be complete and accurate, so correcting inaccurate or incomplete source data must be done there. For example, if you created a Power BI report that is connected to Dynamics 365 for Sales as the live data source, you would have to make any corrections to the data in Dynamics 365 for Sales.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p365">進行這些變更之後，您可以利用[排定的資料重新整理](/power-bi/refresh-scheduled-refresh)功能，來更新儲存在 Power BI 的資料集，以便修訂後的資料會反映在相依 Power BI 資產中。為了符合 GDPR 需求，您應該具有適當的原則，以確保您以適當的韻律重新整理您的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p365">After those changes are made, you can take advantage of the [scheduled data refresh](/power-bi/refresh-scheduled-refresh) capabilities to update the dataset that is stored in Power BI so that the revised data is reflected in the dependent Power BI assets. To help comply with GDPR requirements, you should have policies in place to ensure that you are refreshing your data at an appropriate cadence.</span></span>

### <a name="making-changes-to-content-in-yammer"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1362">對 Yammer 中的內容進行變更</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1362">Making changes to content in Yammer</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p366">針對訊息，使用者可以編輯特定訊息，來修正任何不精確之處。他們可以向 Yammer 驗證管理員要求其所有訊息的清單，然後選取檔案中的連結，檢閱每一個訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p366">For messages, a user can edit a given message to rectify any inaccuracies. They can request a list of all their messages from a Yammer verified admin, and then select a link in the file to review each message.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p367">針對檔案，使用者可以編輯特定檔案，來修正任何不精確之處。他們可以向 Yammer 經驗證的系統管理員要求其所張貼之所有檔案的清單，然後在 Yammer 中存取檔案。透過編號來搜尋檔案，即可檢視匯出至 [檔案] 資料夾的檔案。例如，對於匯出中名為 12345678.ppx 的檔案，請在 Yammer 中使用搜尋方塊搜尋 1235678.ppx。或者，移至 <strong>https://www.yammer.com/\<network\_name\>/\#/files/\<file\_number\></strong>；例如，<strong>https://www.yammer.com/contosomkt.onmicrosoft.com/\#/files/12345678</strong>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p367">For files, a user can edit a given file to rectify any inaccuracies. They can request a list of all the files they posted from a Yammer verified admin, and then access the files in Yammer. Files that are exported into the Files folder can be viewed by searching for the file by number. For example, for a file named 12345678.ppx in the export, use the Search box in Yammer to search for 1235678.ppx. Or, go to <strong>https://www.yammer.com/\<network\_name\>/\#/files/\<file\_number\></strong>; for example, <strong>https://www.yammer.com/contosomkt.onmicrosoft.com/\#/files/12345678</strong>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1370">對於使用者可以透過其設定檔和設定存取的資料，使用者可以進行任何需要的變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1370">For data that the user can access through their profile and settings, the user can make any needed changes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1371">使用者的設定檔：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1371">The user's profile:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p368">如果使用者具有 Yammer 身分識別，使用者可以完全控制其設定檔。如需怎樣檢視和修改設定檔的相關資訊，請參閱[變更我的 Yammer 設定檔和設定](https://support.office.com/article/change-my-yammer-profile-and-settings-a3aeca0e-de34-4897-9b59-de6516542851)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p368">If the user has a Yammer identity, the user has full control of their profile. For information on how to view and modify the profile, see [Change my Yammer profile and settings](https://support.office.com/article/change-my-yammer-profile-and-settings-a3aeca0e-de34-4897-9b59-de6516542851).</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1374">如果使用者具有 Office 365 身分識別，系統會自動從 Office 365 帶入 Yammer 使用者設定檔；這會從 Azure Active Directory (AAD) 取得設定檔資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1374">If the user has an Office 365 identity, the Yammer user profile is pulled automatically from Office 365, which gets the profile information from Azure Active Directory (AAD).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1375">Yammer 使用者可以暫時變更自己在 Yammer 的設定檔；但在 AAD 中發生變更時，會覆寫前者，因此最好在 AAD 中檢視和變更目錄資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1375">Yammer users can temporarily change their profiles in Yammer, but these changes are overwritten when there is a change in AAD, so the best place to view and change directory data is AAD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1376">使用者需要要求系統管理員更新其 AAD。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1376">The user needs to request that AAD be updated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1377">請參閱[從 Office 365 跨其生命週期管理 Yammer 使用者](/yammer/manage-yammer-users/manage-users-across-their-lifecycle)和[新增或變更 Azure Active Directory 中使用者的設定檔資訊](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-users-profile-azure-portal)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1377">See [Manage Yammer users across their lifecycle from Office 365](/yammer/manage-yammer-users/manage-users-across-their-lifecycle) and [Add or change profile information for a user in Azure Active Directory](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-users-profile-azure-portal).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1378">使用者的設定：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1378">The user's settings:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p370">使用者可以變更自己的設定。如需怎樣檢視和修改使用者設定的相關資訊，請參閱[變更我的 Yammer 設定檔和設定](https://support.office.com/article/change-my-yammer-profile-and-settings-a3aeca0e-de34-4897-9b59-de6516542851)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p370">The user can change their own settings. For information on how to view and modify user settings, see [Change my Yammer profile and settings](https://support.office.com/article/change-my-yammer-profile-and-settings-a3aeca0e-de34-4897-9b59-de6516542851).</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p371">使用者的群組成員資格、加上書籤的訊息、追蹤的使用者，以及追蹤的主題。使用者可以變更此資訊。請參閱[在 Yammer 中保持井然有序的提示](https://support.office.com/article/tips-for-staying-organized-in-yammer-40ae9666-75c0-4254-a84c-d87a9542f380)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p371">The user's group membership, bookmarked messages, followed users, and followed topics. The user can change this information; see [Tips for staying organized in Yammer](https://support.office.com/article/tips-for-staying-organized-in-yammer-40ae9666-75c0-4254-a84c-d87a9542f380).</span></span>

## <a name="responding-to-dsr-restriction-requests"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1383">回應 DSR 限制要求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1383">Responding to DSR restriction requests</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1384">以下是限制處理 Office 365 中資料的方式：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1384">Here are the ways to restrict the processing of data in Office 365:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1385">移除 Office 365 應用程式授權，以防止使用者透過應用程式存取資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1385">Remove an Office 365 application license to prevent users from accessing data via an application</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1386">防止使用者存取其商務用 OneDrive 帳戶</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1386">Prevent users from accessing their OneDrive for Business account</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1387">關閉 Office 365 服務，不處理資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1387">Turn off an Office 365 service from processing the data</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1388">暫時移除 SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 中的資料，並保留在內部部署</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1388">Temporarily remove the data from SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business and retain it on-premises</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1389">暫時限制對 SharePoint Online 網站的所有存取</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1389">Temporarily restrict all access to a SharePoint Online site</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1390">防止使用者登入 Office 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1390">Prevent a user from signing in to Office 365</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1391">如果貴組織稍後決定限制不再適用，您可以反轉採取限制的步驟來結束限制；例如，重新指派授權、再次開啟服務，或允許使用者登入 Office 365。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1391">If your organization determines later that a restriction no longer applies, you can end the restriction by reversing the steps you took to restrict it; such as reassigning licenses, turning a service back on, or allowing a user to sign in to Office 365.</span></span>

### <a name="removing-the-license-for-an-office-365-application"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1392">移除 Office 365 應用程式的授權</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1392">Removing the license for an Office 365 application</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1393">如同先前所述，根據預設，貴組織商務用 Microsoft 365 訂閱中包含的所有 Office 365 應用程式的授權已指派給所有使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1393">As previously explained, licenses for all Office 365 applications that are included in your organization's Microsoft 365 for business subscription are assigned to all users by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1394">必要時，若要限制存取受制於 DSR 的資料，IT 系統管理員可以使用 Office 365 系統管理員入口網站，暫時關閉使用者對某應用程式的授權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1394">If necessary to restrict,  access to data that's subject to a DSR, an IT admin can use the Office 365 admin portal temporarily turn off a user's license for an application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1395">如果使用者隨後嘗試使用該應用程式，則他們將會收到未授權的產品通知或他們不會再有權存取的訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1395">If a user then tries to use that application, they'll receive an unlicensed product notification or a message saying they no longer have access.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1396">如需詳細資料，請參閱[從商務用 Office 365 中的使用者移除授權](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/delete-a-user)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1396">For details, see [Remove licenses from users in Office 365 for business](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/delete-a-user).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1397">**注意：**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1397">**Notes:**</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1398">若要限制使用者存取 Yammer，首先您必須[強制執行 Yammer 使用者的 Office 365 身分識別](/yammer/configure-your-yammer-network/enforce-office-365-identity)，然後移除使用者的 Yammer 授權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1398">To restrict a user from accessing Yammer, you must first [enforce Office 365 identify for a Yammer user](/yammer/configure-your-yammer-network/enforce-office-365-identity) and then remove the user's Yammer license.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1399">對於利用 Power BI Embedded 的案例，您可以限制存取內嵌內容的獨立軟體廠商 (ISV) 應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1399">For scenarios that take advantage of Power BI Embedded, you can restrict access to the independent software vendor (ISV) application that the content is embedded in.</span></span>

### <a name="preventing-users-from-accessing-their-onedrive-for-business-account"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1400">防止使用者存取其商務用 OneDrive 帳戶</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1400">Preventing users from accessing their OneDrive for Business account</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1401">移除使用者的 SharePoint Online 授權，並無法防止使用者存取其商務用 OneDrive 帳戶 (若已存在的話)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1401">Removing a user's SharePoint Online license won't prevent them from accessing their OneDrive for Business account if it exists.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1402">您必須移除使用者對其商務用 OneDrive 帳戶的權限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1402">You have to remove the user's permissions to their OneDrive for Business account to.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1403">做法為以其商務用 OneDrive 帳戶的網站集合擁有者身分移除使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1403">You can do this by removing the user as a site collection owner of their OneDrive for Business account.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1404">具體來說，您必須從其使用者設定檔中的主要網站集合系統管理員網站集合系統管理員「主要網站集合管理員」和「網站集合管理員」群組中移除使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1404">Specifically, you have to remove the user from the Primary Site Collection Administrator and Site Collection Administrators groups in their user profile.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1405">請參閱[管理 SharePoint 管理中心的使用者設定檔](/sharepoint/manage-user-profiles)中的＜新增和移除商務用 OneDrive 帳戶上的系統管理員＞一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1405">See the "Add and remove admins on a OneDrive for Business account" section in [Manage user profiles in the SharePoint admin center](/sharepoint/manage-user-profiles).</span></span>

### <a name="turning-off-an-office-365-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1406">關閉 Office 365 服務</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1406">Turning off an Office 365 Service</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p374">解決 DSR 要求來限制處理資料的另一種方法，就是是關閉 Office 365 服務。這會影響整個組織中的所有使用者，並防止每個人使用服務，或存取服務中的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p374">Another way to address a DSR request to restrict the processing of data is to turn off an Office 365 service. This impacts all users in your entire organization and prevents everyone from using the service or accessing data in the service.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p375">關閉服務最方便的方式是使用 Office 365 PowerShell，並從組織中的所有使用者移除對應的使用者授權。這會實際上限制任何人存取該服務中的資料。如需詳細指示，請參閱[使用 Office 365 PowerShell 停用服務的存取](/microsoft-365/enterprise/disable-access-to-services-with-microsoft-365-powershell)，並遵循程序從單一授權方案停用使用者的 Office 365 服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p375">The most expedient way to turn off a service is to use Office 365 PowerShell and remove the corresponding user license from all users in the organization. This will in effect restrict anyone from access data in that service. For detailed instructions, see [Disable access to services with Office 365 PowerShell](/microsoft-365/enterprise/disable-access-to-services-with-microsoft-365-powershell) and follow the procedures to disable Office 365 services for users from a single licensing plan.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p376">針對 Yammer，除了從使用者帳戶中移除 Yammer 授權之外，您也必須將使用者使用 Yammer 認證登入 Yammer 的能力停用 (透過在登入時，強制使用 Office 365 認證)。如需詳細指示，請參閱[關閉 Microsoft 365 使用者的 Yammer 存取](https://support.office.com/article/Turn-off-Yammer-access-for-Office-365-users-1f79bfad-f713-4143-aa5d-5584985ce53a)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p376">For Yammer, in additional to removing the Yammer license from user accounts, you also must disable users' ability to sign in to Yammer with Yammer credentials (by enforcing the use of their Office 365 credentials when signing in). For detailed instructions, see [Turn off Yammer access for Microsoft 365 users](https://support.office.com/article/Turn-off-Yammer-access-for-Office-365-users-1f79bfad-f713-4143-aa5d-5584985ce53a).</span></span>

### <a name="temporarily-removing-data-from-sharepoint-online-or-onedrive-for-business-sites"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1414">暫時從 SharePoint Online 或商務用 OneDrive 網站中移除資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1414">Temporarily removing data from SharePoint Online or OneDrive for Business sites</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p377">限制處理個人資料的另一種方法，就是暫時從 Office 365 DSR 中移除它，以回應 DSR。當貴組織決定限制不再適用時，您可以將資料匯回至 Office 365。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p377">Another way to restrict the processing of personal data is to temporarily remove it from Office 365 in response to a DSR. When your organization determines that the restriction no longer applies, you can import the data back into Office 365.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1417">因為大部分 Office 文件位於 SharePoint Online 或商務用 OneDrive 網站，以下是從網站中移除文件，然後重新匯入的高層級程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1417">Because most Office documents are on a SharePoint Online or OneDrive for Business site, here's a high-level process for removing documents from sites and then re-importing them.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p378">取得作為限制要求主體的文件複本。您可能必須要求存取網站，或要求全域管理員或網站集合系統管理員提供您文件的複本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p378">Get a copy of the document that is the subject of the restriction request. You may have to request either access to the site or ask a global admin or a site collection administrator to provide you with a copy of the document.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1420">將文件儲存在內部部署位置 (例如檔案伺服器或檔案共用) 中，或 Microsoft 雲端中 Office 365 租用戶以外的另一個位置中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1420">Store the document in an on-premises location (such as a file server or a file share) or another location other than your Office 365 tenant in the Microsoft cloud.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p379">從 Office 365 中永久刪除 (清除) 原始文件。這是 3 步驟的程序：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p379">Permanently delete (purge) the original document from Office 365. This is a 3-step process:</span></span>

   1.  <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1423">刪除文件的原始複本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1423">Delete the original copy of the document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1424">當您從網站中刪除文件時，此文件會傳送至 [資源回收筒] (又稱為 *第一階段資源回收筒*)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1424">When you delete a document from a site, it's sent to the site Recycle Bin (also called the *first-stage Recycle Bin*).</span></span>

   1.  <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1425">移至網站 [資源回收筒]，然後刪除該文件複本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1425">Go to the site Recycle Bin and delete that copy of the document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1426">當您從網站 [資源回收筒] 中刪除文件時，此文件會傳送至網站集合 [資源回收筒] (又稱為 *第二階段資源回收筒*)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1426">When you delete a document from the site Recycle Bin, it's sent to the site collection Recycle Bin (also called the *second-stage Recycle Bin*).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1427">請參閱 [從 SharePoint 文件庫中刪除檔案、資料夾或連結](https://support.microsoft.com/office/delete-a-file-folder-or-link-from-a-sharepoint-document-library-71f3c90a-0d24-4d80-8b66-f88234b79a52)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1427">See [Delete a file, folder, or link from a SharePoint document library](https://support.microsoft.com/office/delete-a-file-folder-or-link-from-a-sharepoint-document-library-71f3c90a-0d24-4d80-8b66-f88234b79a52).</span></span>

   1.  <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1428">移至網站集合 [資源回收筒]，然後刪除該文件複本，這會從 Office 365 中永久將其移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1428">Go to the site collection Recycle Bin and delete that copy of the document, which permanently removes it from Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1429">請參閱 [從網站集合資源回收筒中刪除項目](https://support.microsoft.com/office/delete-items-from-the-site-collection-recycle-bin-dd5c00c2-aef6-4458-9d04-80b185077653)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1429">See [Delete items from the site collection recycle bin](https://support.microsoft.com/office/delete-items-from-the-site-collection-recycle-bin-dd5c00c2-aef6-4458-9d04-80b185077653).</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1430">當限制不再適用時，已儲存在內部部署的文件複本可以重新上傳至 Office 365 中的網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1430">When the restriction no longer applies, the copy of the document that was stored on-premises can be re-uploaded to the site in Office 365.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p383">如果文件位於處於保留狀態的網站 (具有 Office 365 的其中一個保留或法務保存措施功能)，則先前程序無法運作。在 DSR 限制要求的優先權高於法務保存措施的情況下，您必須先從網站中移除保留，然後才能永久刪除文件。此外，這也會永久移除已刪除文件的文件歷程記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p383">The preceding procedure won't work if the document is located on a site that is on hold (with one of the retention or legal hold features in Office 365). In the case where a restriction request for a DSR takes precedence over a legal hold, the hold would have to be removed from the site before a document could be permanently deleted. Additionally, the document history for deleted documents is permanently removed.</span></span>

### <a name="temporarily-restricting-access-to-sharepoint-online-sites"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1434">暫時限制存取 SharePoint Online 網站</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1434">Temporarily restricting access to SharePoint Online sites</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1435">SharePoint Online 系統管理員可以鎖定網站集合來暫時防止所有使用者存取 SharePoint Online 網站集合 (透過使用 SharePoint Online PowerShell 中的 **Set-sposite LockState** 命令)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1435">A SharePoint Online administrator can temporarily prevent all users from accessing a SharePoint Online site collection by locking the site collection (by using the **Set-SPOSite -LockState** command in SharePoint Online PowerShell).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1436">這會防止使用者存取網站集合，以及位於該網站的任何內容或資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1436">This prevents users for accessing the site collection and any content or data that's located in the site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1437">如果您隨後判斷使用者應該能夠存取網站，系統管理員可以解除鎖定網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1437">If you then determine that users should be able to access the site, the administrator can unlock the site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1438">如需執行此 PowerShell Cmdlet 的相關資訊，請參閱 [Set-SPOSite](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/set-sposite)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1438">See [Set-SPOSite](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/set-sposite) for information about running this PowerShell cmdlet.</span></span>

### <a name="preventing-a-user-from-signing-in-to-office-365"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1439">防止使用者登入 Office 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1439">Preventing a user from signing in to Office 365</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p385">IT 系統管理員也可以防止使用者登入 Office 365，這會防止使用者存取任何 Office 365 線上服務，或處理儲存在 Office 365 中的任何資料。請參閱[封鎖離職員工對 Office 365 資料的存取](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/remove-former-employee)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p385">An IT admin can also prevent a user from signing into Office 365, which would prevent the user from accessing any Office 365 online service or processing any data stored in Office 365. See [Block a former employee's access to Office 365 data](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/remove-former-employee).</span></span>

## <a name="part-2-responding-to-dsrs-with-respect-to-insights-generated-by-office-365"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1442">第 2 部分：按照 Office 365 產生的見解來回應 DSR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1442">Part 2: Responding to DSRs with Respect to Insights Generated by Office 365</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1443">Microsoft Office 365 服務套件包含線上服務，可對已選擇使用服務的使用者和組織提供見解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1443">The Microsoft suite of Office 365 services includes online services that provide insights to users and organizations that have opted to use them.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1444">Delve 和 MyAnalytics 可提供見解給個別使用者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1444">Delve and MyAnalytics provide insights to individual users</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1445">工作場所分析可提供見解給組織。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1445">Workplace Analytics provides insights to organizations.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1446">下列各節描述這些服務：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1446">These services are described in the following sections:</span></span>

### <a name="delve"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1447">Delve</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1447">Delve</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1448">在 Delve 中，使用者可以管理其 Office 365 設定檔，並探索人員以及與他們相關的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1448">In Delve, users can manage their Office 365 profile and discover people and documents that may be relevant to them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1449">使用者只能看到他們有權存取的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1449">Users can only see documents that they have access to.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1450">如需一系列有關 Delve 的有用文件，請參閱 [Microsoft Delve](https://support.office.com/article/What-is-Office-Delve-1315665a-c6af-4409-a28d-49f8916878ca)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1450">For a series of helpful articles about Delve, see [Office Delve](https://support.office.com/article/What-is-Office-Delve-1315665a-c6af-4409-a28d-49f8916878ca).</span></span>

#### <a name="access-and-export"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1451">存取及匯出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1451">Access and export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p387">系統管理員無法存取或匯出使用者的 Delve 資料。這表示，使用者必須自行存取和匯出 Delve 資料。這些資料類型大多可讓使用者直接從 Delve 存取和匯出，但某些資料類型只能透過其他服務來使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p387">Admins can't access or export a users' Delve data. This means that users have to access and export Delve data themselves. Most of the data types can be accessed and exported directly from Delve, but some data types are only available through other services.</span></span>

##### <a name="data-available-in-the-delve-user-interface"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1455">可在 Delve 使用者介面中使用的資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1455">Data available in the Delve user interface</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1456">**設定檔資料：** 這是來自貴組織 Azure Active Directory 中全域通訊清單的設定檔資訊，以及使用者選擇新增有關本身的選擇性資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1456">**Profile data:** This is the profile information from your organization's Global Address List in Azure Active Directory, and optional information that users have chosen to add about themselves.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1457">若要存取或匯出 Delve 中的設定檔資料，使用者可以選取 [我 **]** \> [更新設定檔 **]**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1457">To access or export profile data in Delve, a user can select **Me** \> **Update profile**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1458">他們可以直接從頁面複製內容，或</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1458">They can either copy the content directly from the page or</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1459">**部落格資料：** 這是使用者發佈的部落格文章。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1459">**Blog data:** This is blog posts published by a user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1460">若要存取或匯出部落格資料，使用者可以選取 [我 **]** \> [所有文章 **]**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1460">To access or export blog data, a user can select **Me** \> **All posts**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1461">他們可以直接從頁面複製內容，或取得螢幕擷取畫面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1461">They can either copy the content directly from the page or take a screenshot.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1462">**最近的人員資料：** 這些是組織中 Delve 所推斷在指定時間與使用者最相關的人員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1462">**Recent people data:** These are the people in the organization that Delve has inferred are most relevant to the user at a given time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1463">當使用者在 [選取人員以查看他們正在處理的項目] 窗格中選取 [我 **]** \> [查看全部 **]** 時，Delve 會顯示特定時間使用者的最相關人員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1463">When a user selects **Me** \> **See all** in the "select a person to see what they're working on" pane, Delve shows the most relevant people for a user at a given time.</span></span>

##### <a name="data-available-through-an-export-link-in-delve"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1464">可透過 Delve 中的匯出連結提供的資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1464">Data available through an export link in Delve</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p391">**人員清單資料：** 這些是使用者已在 Delve 中檢視的人員。**[人員]** 清單會顯示在首頁的左窗格中。使用者可以匯出他們最近在 Delve 中檢視的人員清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p391">**People list data:** These are the people the user has viewed in Delve. The **People** list is shown in the left pane on the home page. Users can export the list of people they have most recently viewed in Delve.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p392">**我的最愛資料：** 以下是使用者已標示為我的最愛的討論區和文件。**[我的最愛]** 頁面會顯示使用者已新增至我的最愛的討論區和文件。使用者可以匯出其目前我的最愛討論區和文件的清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p392">**Favorites data:** These are boards and documents that the user has marked as their favorite. The **Favorites** page shows boards and documents that the user has added to their favorites. Users can export a list of their current favorite boards and documents.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p393">**功能設定資料：** 這些是使用者使用 Delve 所產生的設定或動作。使用者可以匯出這些設定的完整清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p393">**Feature settings data:** These are Delve configurations or actions that result from a user's use of Delve. Users can export a full list of these settings.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1473">若要存取或匯出上述資料，使用者可以選取 Delve 右上角的齒輪圖示，然後選取 [功能設定 **]**  >  [匯出資料 **]**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1473">To access or export the above data, the user can select the gear icon in the upper-right corner in Delve, and then select **Feature settings** > **Export data**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1474">資訊會以 JSON 格式匯出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1474">Information is exported in JSON format.</span></span>

##### <a name="data-thats-available-through-other-services"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1475">可透過其他服務提供的資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1475">Data that's available through other services</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1476">**熱門文件資料：** 這些是可能與使用者相關的文件和電子郵件附件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1476">**Popular documents data:** These are documents and email attachments that may be relevant to the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1477">Delve 會根據使用者的活動，以及他們在 Office 365 中往來的人員，動態組織這些文件和電子郵件訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1477">Delve dynamically organizes these documents and email messages based on the user's activities and people they work with in Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1478">當使用者開啟 Delve，或選取 [首頁 **]** 時，Delve 會顯示特定時間使用者的最相關文件或附件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1478">When a user opens Delve or selects **Home**, Delve shows the most relevant documents or attachments for the user at a given time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1479">若要存取或匯出實際的文件和附件，使用者可以移至已透過其提供文件或附件的 Office 365 服務 (例如 Office.com、SharePoint Online、商務用 OneDrive 或 Exchange Online)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1479">To access or export the actual documents and attachments, the user can go to the Office 365 service through which the document or attachment was made available (such as Office.com, SharePoint Online, OneDrive for Business, or Exchange Online).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1480">**最近的文件和電子郵件附件資料：** 這些是使用者所修改的最新文件和電子郵件附件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1480">**Recent documents and email attachments data:** These are the most recent documents and email attachments that the user has modified.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1481">當使用者在 [回到您最近的文件和電子郵件附件] 窗格中選取 [我 **]** \> [查看全部 **]** 時，Delve 會顯示使用者在特定時間修改的最新文件和電子郵件附件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1481">When a user selects **Me** \> **See all** in the "Get back to your recent documents and email attachments" pane, Delve shows the latest documents and email attachments the user has modified at a given time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1482">若要存取或匯出實際的文件和附件，使用者可以移至已透過其提供文件或附件的 Office 365 服務，例如 Office.com、SharePoint Online、商務用 OneDrive 或 Exchange Online。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1482">To access or export the actual documents and attachments, the user can go to the Office 365 service through which the document or attachment was made available; for example, Office.com, SharePoint Online, OneDrive for Business, or Exchange Online.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1483">**來自您周圍人員資料的文件：** 這些是 Delve 所推斷在特定時間與使用者最相關的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1483">**Documents from people around your data:** These are the documents that Delve has inferred are most relevant to the user at a given time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1484">當使用者在 [探索來自您周遭人員的文件] 窗格中選取 [我 **]** \> [查看全部 **]** 時，Delve 會顯示特定時間使用者的最相關文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1484">When a user selects **Me** \> **See all** in the "Discover documents from people around you" pane, Delve shows the most relevant documents for a user at a given time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1485">若要存取或匯出實際的文件，使用者可以移至已透過其提供文件或附件的 Office 365 服務 (例如 Office.com、SharePoint Online、商務用 OneDrive 或 Exchange Online)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1485">To access or export the actual documents, the user can go to the Office 365 service through which the document or attachment was made available (for example, Office.com, SharePoint Online, OneDrive for Business, or Exchange Online).</span></span>

#### <a name="rectify"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1486">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1486">Rectify</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1487">使用者可以修改 Delve 中的下列資訊：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1487">Users can modify the following information in Delve:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1488">**設定檔資訊：** 使用者可以選取 [我 **]** \>[更新設定檔 **]**，來更新其資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1488">**Profile information:** A user can select **Me** \> **Update profile** to update their information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1489">根據貴組織的全域通訊清單中的設定，使用者可能無法修改所有設定檔資訊，例如其名稱或職稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1489">Depending on your organization's settings in the Global Address List, users may not be able to modify all their profile information, such as their name or job title.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1490">**功能設定：** 使用者可以選取 Delve 右上角的齒輪圖示，然後選取 [功能設定 **]** \>來變更所需的設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1490">**Feature settings:** A user can select the gear icon in the upper-right corner in Delve, and then select **Feature settings** \> to change the desired settings.</span></span>

#### <a name="restrict"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1491">限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1491">Restrict</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p399">若要針對貴組織限制 Delve 中的處理，您可以關閉 Office Graph。如需深入了解，請參閱[這裡](/sharepoint/delve-for-office-365-admins)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p399">To restrict processing in Delve for your organization, you can turn off the Office Graph. Learn more [here](/sharepoint/delve-for-office-365-admins).</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1494">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1494">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1495">使用者可以刪除 Delve 中的下列資訊：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1495">Users can delete the following information in Delve:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1496">**設定檔資訊：** 若要刪除設定檔資訊，使用者可以選取 [我 **]** \> [更新設定檔 **]**，來刪除自由格式文字。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1496">**Profile information:** To delete profile information, a user can select **Me** \> **Update profile** and either delete free-form text.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1497">根據組織的全域通訊清單中的設定，使用者可能無法刪除其所有設定檔資訊，例如其名稱或工作職稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1497">Depending on your organization's settings in the Global Address List, users may not be able to delete all their profile information, such as their name or job title.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1498">**文件和電子郵件附件：** 若要刪除文件或附件，使用者必須移至儲存文件或附件的服務 (例如 SharePoint Online、商務用 OneDrive，或 Exchange Online)，並刪除那裡的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1498">**Documents and email attachments:** To delete a document or attachment, users must go to the service where the document or attachment is stored (such as SharePoint Online, OneDrive for Business, or Exchange Online) and delete the document there.</span></span>

### <a name="myanalytics"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1499">MyAnalytics</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1499">MyAnalytics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1500">MyAnalytics 會提供統計資料，以協助使用者了解其工作時間分配情況。  </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1500">MyAnalytics provides statistics to users to help them understand how they spend their time at work.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1501">若要協助您的使用者深入了解在其個人儀表板中呈現給他們的資料，以及資料的計算方式，請將您的使用者導向至 [MyAnalytics 個人儀表板](/workplace-analytics/myanalytics/use/dashboard-2)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1501">To help your users better understand the data that is presented to them in their personal dashboard and how that data is calculated, direct your users to [MyAnalytics personal dashboard](/workplace-analytics/myanalytics/use/dashboard-2).</span></span>

#### <a name="access-and-export"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1502">存取及匯出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1502">Access and export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1503">如果您的組織使用 MyAnalytics，則 Microsoft 會為所有使用者產生見解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1503">If your organization uses MyAnalytics, then Microsoft generates insights for all users.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1504">MyAnalytics 的所有見解都衍生自使用者信箱中的電子郵件和會議標題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1504">All MyAnalytics insights are derived from email and meeting headers in the user's mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1505">Microsoft 讓您能夠在安全性與合規性中心使用 DSR 案例工具，匯出 MyAnalytics 用來產生這些見解的資料。如需詳細指示，請參閱[從 MyAnalytics 和 Office 漫遊服務匯出資料](https://delve.office.com)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1505">Users can go to the [MyAnalytics dashboard](https://delve.office.com) while signed in to their Office 365 account to view the insights that are generated about how they spend their time at work.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1506">如果他們想要擁有其資訊的永久複本，他們可以製作 MyAnalytics 見解的螢幕擷取畫面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1506">They can take screenshots of MyAnalytics insights if they want to have permanent copies of their information.</span></span>

#### <a name="rectify"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1507">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1507">Rectify</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p403">MyAnalytics 所產生的所有見解都是衍生自使用者的郵件和行事曆項目。因此，除了來源電子郵件或行事曆項目外，沒有要修正的項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p403">All insights generated by MyAnalytics are derived from the user's mail and calendar items. Therefore, there is nothing to rectify other than the source email or calendar items.</span></span>

#### <a name="restrict"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1510">限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1510">Restrict</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p404">若要限制特定使用者的處理，您可以從 MyAnalytics 排除它們。若要查看如何進行，請參閱[設定 MyAnalytics 使用者設定](/workplace-analytics/myanalytics/setup/configure-myanalytics)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p404">To restrict processing for a specific user, you can opt them out of MyAnalytics. To see how, see [Configure MyAnalytics user settings](/workplace-analytics/myanalytics/setup/configure-myanalytics).</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1513">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1513">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p405">從 Active Directory 中「實刪除」使用者帳戶時，會清除所有信箱內容，包括 MyAnalytics 資料。如需詳細資訊，請參閱本指南的[刪除使用者](#deleting-a-user)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p405">All mailbox content, including MyAnalytics data, is purged when a user account is "hard-deleted" from Active Directory. For more information, see the [Deleting a user](#deleting-a-user) section in this guide.</span></span>

### <a name="workplace-analytics"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1516">工作場所分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1516">Workplace Analytics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p406">「工作場所分析」可讓組織利用其自己的商務資料來擴增 Office 365 資料，以深入了解組織生產力、共同作業模式和員工參與度。[本文](/workplace-analytics/index-orig)說明了貴組織對工作場所分析處理的資料所具有的控制權，以及誰有權存取該資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p406">Workplace Analytics allows organizations to augment Office 365 data with their own business data to gain insights about organizational productivity, collaboration patterns, and employee engagement. [This article](/workplace-analytics/index-orig) explains the control that your organization has over the data that Workplace Analytics processes and who has access to that data.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1519">為了協助在工作場所分析中使用 DSR：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1519">To assist you with DSRs in Workplace Analytics:</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p407">請判斷貴組織是否使用「工作場所分析」。如需詳細資訊，請參閱[將授權指派給使用者](/microsoft-365/admin/manage/assign-licenses-to-users)。如果您的組織並未使用「工作場所分析」，則不需採取進一步動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p407">Determine whether your organization is using Workplace Analytics. For more information, see [Assign licenses to users](/microsoft-365/admin/manage/assign-licenses-to-users). If your organization is not using Workplace Analytics, there is no further action.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p408">如果貴組織使用「工作場所分析」，接著請查看貴組織中誰被指派工作場所分析系統管理員的角色。您也應該判斷資料主體的信箱是否有「工作場所分析」的授權。如有需要，讓工作場所分析系統管理員在處理下列 DSR 要求時連絡 Microsoft 支援服務：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p408">If your organization is using Workplace Analytics, then see who in your organization has been assigned to the role of Workplace Analytics administrator. You should also determine if the data subject's mailbox is licensed for Workplace Analytics. If necessary, have your Workplace Analytics administrator contact Microsoft Support in handling the following DSR requests:</span></span> 

#### <a name="access-and-export"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1526">存取及匯出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1526">Access and export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p409">您所建立的「工作場所分析」報告中的見解不一定包含貴組織已對「工作場所分析」授權之使用者的個人資料，視貴組織用來補充 Office 365 資料的資訊而定。您的工作場所分析系統管理員必須檢閱這些報告，才能判斷它們是否包含使用者的個人資料。如果報告的確包含使用者的個人資料，則您必須決定是否要提供該報告的複本給使用者。「工作場所分析」可讓您匯出報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p409">Workplace Analytics insight reports created by you may or may not contain personal data of users that your organization licensed for Workplace Analytics, depending on the information that your organization used to supplement the Office 365 data. Your Workplace Analytics administrator needs to review those reports to determine if they contain a user's personal data. If a report does contain a user's personal data, then you need to decide if you want to provide a copy of that report to the user. Workplace Analytics allows you to export the report.</span></span> 

#### <a name="rectify"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1531">修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1531">Rectify</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p410">如上所述，「工作場所分析」會使用 Office 365 資料與您提供的組織資料，來產生您有興趣的報告。無法修正 Office 365 資料；這取決於使用者的電子郵件和行事曆活動。不過，您可以修正已上傳至「工作場所分析」以便產生報告的組織資料。若要這麼做，您必須修正來源資料、上傳，然後重新執行報告，來產生新的「工作場所分析」報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p410">As explained above, Workplace Analytics uses Office 365 data with the organizational data that you provide to generate reports of interest to you. The Office 365 data can't be rectified; it's based on a user's email and calendar activities. However, the organizational data that you have uploaded into Workplace Analytics to generate the report can be rectified.
