To do this, you need to correct the source data, upload it, and rerun the report to generate a new Workplace Analytics report.</span></span>

#### <a name="restrict"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1536">限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1536">Restrict</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1537">若要限制特定使用者的處理，您可以移除他們的「工作場所分析」授權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1537">To restrict processing for a specific user, you can remove their Workplace Analytics license.</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1538">刪除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1538">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p411">如果想要從一或多份「工作場所分析」報告中移除資料主體，您可以刪除該報告。您需負責從您用來產生報告的任何組織資料中刪除使用者，並且重新上傳資料。從 Azure Active Directory 中「實刪除」使用者帳戶時，就會移除有關使用者的所有資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p411">If a data subject would like to be removed from a Workplace Analytics report or set of reports, you can delete the report. It is your responsibility to delete users from any organizational data that you used to generate the report, and reupload the data. All data about the user is removed when a user account is "hard-deleted" from Azure Active Directory.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1542">若要移除資料主體的個人資料，全域系統管理員可以執行下列步驟：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1542">To remove the personal data of a data subject, a global administrator can take the following steps:</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1543">移除資料主體的工作場所分析授權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1543">Remove the Workplace Analytics license from the data subject.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p412">刪除資料主體的 Azure Active Directory (AAD) 項目。(如需詳細資訊，請參閱[刪除使用者](/azure/active-directory/fundamentals/add-users-azure-active-directory#delete-a-user)。)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p412">Delete the Azure Active Directory (AAD) entry for the data subject. (For more information, see [Delete a user](/azure/active-directory/fundamentals/add-users-azure-active-directory#delete-a-user).)</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p413">連絡支援人員並請支援人員為資料主體權限 (DSR) 使用者刪除要求開啟票證。在此票證中，使用資料主體的使用者主要名稱 (UPN) 來識別資料主體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p413">Contact support and have support open a ticket for a Data Subject Rights (DSR) user-delete request. In this ticket, identify the data subject by using their User Principal Name (UPN).</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1548">從公司的人力資源系統匯出人力資源資料複本 (請參閱[匯出資料](/workplace-analytics/setup/prepare-organizational-data))，從該人力資源資料檔案中移除資料主體的資訊，然後將已編輯的 .csv 格式人力資源資料檔案上傳到工作場所分析 (請參閱[上傳組織資料](/workplace-analytics/setup/upload-organizational-data))。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1548">Export a copy of the HR data from the company's HR system (see [Export data](/workplace-analytics/setup/prepare-organizational-data)), remove the data subject's information from that HR data file, and then upload the edited HR data file in .csv format into Workplace Analytics (see [Upload organizational data](/workplace-analytics/setup/upload-organizational-data)).</span></span>

## <a name="part-3-responding-to-dsrs-for-system-generated-logs"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1549">第 3 部分：回應系統所產生記錄的 DSR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1549">Part 3: Responding to DSRs for system-generated Logs</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p414">Microsoft 也讓您能夠存取、匯出及刪除系統所產生的記錄，根據 GDPR「個人資料」的廣泛定義，這些記錄可能會視為個人資料。系統所產生的記錄中，根據 GDPR可能會視為個人資料的範例包括：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p414">Microsoft also provides you with the ability to access, export, and delete system-generated logs that may be deemed personal under the GDPR's broad definition of "personal data." Examples of system-generated logs that may be deemed personal under GDPR include:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1552">產品和服務使用情況資料 (例如使用者活動記錄)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1552">Product and service usage data such as user activity logs</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1553">使用者搜尋要求和查詢資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1553">User search requests and query data</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1554">作為系統功能與使用者或其他系統互動的產品和服務所產生的資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1554">Data generated by product and services as a product of system functionality and interaction by users or other systems</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p415">系統不支援在系統產生的記錄中限制或修正資料的能力。系統所產生的記錄構成了 Microsoft 雲端中所進行的實際動作和診斷資料，對這類資料的修改會危害動作的歷程記錄，並增加詐騙和安全性風險。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p415">The ability to restrict or rectify data in system-generated logs is not supported. Data in system-generated logs constitutes factual actions conducted within the Microsoft cloud and diagnostic data, and modifications to such data would compromise the historical record of actions and increase fraud and security risks.</span></span>

### <a name="accessing-and-exporting-system-generated-logs"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1557">存取和匯出系統所產生的記錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1557">Accessing and exporting system-generated logs</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p416">租用戶管理員是組織內唯一可以存取與特定使用者使用 Office 365 服務和應用程式相關聯的系統所產生的記錄檔。針對匯出要求所擷取的資料會以機器可讀取的格式提供；且會以檔案的形式提供，讓使用者知道與資料相關聯的是哪些服務。如上所述，所擷取的資料不會包含可能造成安全性或服務穩定性受損的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p416">The tenant admin is the only person within your organization who can access system-generated logs associated with a particular user's use of Office 365 services and applications. The data retrieved for an export request will be provided in a machine-readable format and will be provided in files that will allow the user to know which services the data is associated with. As noted above, the data retrieved will not include data that may compromise the security or stability of the service.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1561">若要存取和匯出系統產生的記錄：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1561">To access and export system-generated logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1562">登入 Azure 入口網站，然後選取 [所有服務]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1562">Sign in to the Azure portal and select **All services**.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1563">在篩選中輸入原則，然後選取 [原則]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1563">Type policy into the filter, and then select **Policy**.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1564">請在 [原則] 刀鋒視窗上，依序選取 [使用者隱私權]、[管理使用者要求]、[新增匯出要求]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1564">In the **Policy** blade, select **User privacy**, select **Manage User Requests**, and then select **Add export request**.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1565">完成 [匯出資料要求]：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1565">Complete the **Export data request**:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p417">**使用者**。請輸入要求匯出的 Azure Active Directory 使用者的電子郵件地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p417">**User**. Type the email address of the Azure Active Directory user that requested the export.</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p418">**訂用帳戶**。請選取用於報告資源使用量和收取服務費用的帳戶。這也是您 Azure 儲存體帳戶的所在位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p418">**Subscription**. Select the account you use to report resource usage and to bill for services. This is also the location of your Azure storage account.</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p419">**儲存體帳戶**。請選取您的 Azure 儲存體 (Blob) 所在的位置。如需詳細資訊，請參閱「Microsoft Azure 儲存體 - Blob 儲存體簡介」文章。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p419">**Storage account**. Select the location of your Azure Storage (Blob). For more info, see the Introduction to Microsoft Azure Storage — Blob storage article.</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p420">**容器**。請建立新的 (或選取現有的) 容器，作為使用者所匯出隱私權資料的儲存位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p420">**Container**. Create a new (or select an existing) container as the storage location for the user's exported privacy data.</span></span>

5. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1576">選取 [建立]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1576">Select **Create**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1577">匯出要求會進入 **擱置** 狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1577">The export request goes into **Pending** status.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1578">您可以在 [使用者隱私權]  >  [概觀] 刀鋒視窗上，檢視報告狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1578">You can view the report status on the **User privacy** > **Overview blade**.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1579">因為個人資料可能來自多個系統，有可能匯出程序需要長達 1 個月才能完成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1579">Because personal data can come from multiple systems, it's possible that the export process might take up to one month to complete.</span></span>

### <a name="notify-about-exporting-or-deleting-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1580">匯出或刪除問題的通知</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1580">Notify about exporting or deleting issues</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1581">如果您從 Azure 入口網站匯出或刪除資料時遇到問題，請前往 Azure 入口網站 **[協助 + 支援]** 刀鋒視窗，並在 **[訂閱管理]** > **[訂閱的隱私權和合規性要求]** > **[隱私權刀鋒視窗和 GDPR 要求]** 下提交新票證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1581">If you run into issues while exporting or deleting data from the Azure portal, go to the Azure portal **Help + Support** blade and submit a new ticket under **Subscription Management** > **Privacy and compliance requests for Subscriptions** > **Privacy Blade and GDPR Requests**.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1582">當您從 Azure 入口網站匯出資料時，少數應用程式的系統產生資料不會匯出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1582">When you export data from the Azure portal, system-generated data for a few applications will not be exported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1583">若要匯出這些應用程式的資料，請參閱[匯出系統所產生記錄資料的其他步驟](/microsoft-365/compliance/gdpr-system-generated-log-data)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1583">To export data for these applications, see [Additional steps to export system-generated log data](/microsoft-365/compliance/gdpr-system-generated-log-data).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1584">下列內容摘要說明系統所產生記錄檔的存取和匯出：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1584">The following summarizes accessing and exporting system-generated logs:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1585">**使用 Azure 入口網站進行匯出要求需要多久時間才能完成要求？：** 視各種因素而定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1585">**How long does an export request using the Azure portal take to complete a request?**: This can depend on several factors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1586">通常應該會在一到兩天內完成，但最多可能需要 30 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1586">Usually it should complete in one or two days, but it can take up to 30 days.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1587">**輸出的格式是什麼？：** 輸出是電腦可讀取的結構化檔案，例如 XML、CSV 或 JSON。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1587">**What format will the output be in?**: The output is structured machine-readable files such as XML, CSV, or JSON.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1588">**誰有權存取 Azure 入口網站，以提交對系統所產生記錄檔的存取要求？**：Office 365 全域系統管理員將有權存取 Azure 入口網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1588">**Who has access to Azure portal to submit access requests for system-generated data?**: Office 365 global administrators have access to the Azure portal.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1589">**匯出結果會傳回哪些資料？**：結果包含 Microsoft 儲存之系統產生的記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1589">**What data do the export results return?**: The results contain system-generated logs that Microsoft stores.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1590">匯出的資料會跨越不同的 Microsoft 服務，包括 Office 365、Azure 和 Dynamics。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1590">Exported data spans across various Microsoft services including Office 365, Azure, and Dynamics.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1591">結果不會包含可能造成服務安全性或穩定性受損的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1591">The results do not include data that may compromise the security or stability of the service.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1592">**資料傳回給使用者的方式為何？**：系統會將資料匯出至貴組織的 Azure 儲存體位置；貴組織的系統管理員將決定是否向使用者顯示此資料，或將此資料傳回給使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1592">**How is data returned to the user?**: Data is exported to your organization's Azure storage location; it's up to admins in your organization to determine how they will show/return this data to users.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1593">**系統產生的記錄資料看起來是什麼樣子？**：以下是 JSON 格式資料的範例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1593">**What will system-generated log data look like?**: Below is an example, the data are in JSON format:</span></span>

    ```JSON
    [{
    "DateTime": "2017-04-28T12:09:29-07:00",
    "AppName": "SharePoint",
    "Action": "OpenFile",
    "IP": "154.192.13.131",
    "DevicePlatform": "Windows 1.0.1607"
    }]
    ```

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p425">您也可以透過搜尋安全性與合規性中心內的 Office 365 稽核記錄，來擷取部分 Microsoft 最多人使用的服務 (例如 Exchange Online、SharePoint Online、商務用 Skype、Yammer 和 Office 365 群組) 的產品和服務使用情況資料。如需詳細資訊，請參閱附錄 A 中的[在 DSR 調查時使用 Office 365 稽核記錄搜尋工具](#use-the-audit-log-search-tool-in-dsr-investigations)。您可能有興趣使用稽核記錄，因為可將權限指派給貴組織中的其他人 (例如您的法務人員) 來搜尋稽核記錄，以存取此資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p425">Product and service usage data for some of Microsoft's most often-used services, such as Exchange Online, SharePoint Online, Skype for Business, Yammer, and Office 365 Groups can also be retrieved by searching the Office 365 audit log in the Security & Compliance Center. For more information, see [Use the Office 365 audit log search tool in DSR investigations](#use-the-audit-log-search-tool-in-dsr-investigations) in Appendix A. Using the audit log may be of interest to you because it's possible to assign permissions to other people in your organization (such as your compliance officer) to search the audit log to access this data.</span></span>

### <a name="deleting-system-generated-logs"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1596">刪除系統產生的記錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1596">Deleting system-generated logs</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p426">若要透過存取要求來刪除系統產生的記錄，您必須將使用者從該服務中移除，並永久刪除其 Azure Active Directory 帳戶。如需永久刪除使用者的相關指示，請參閱本指南中[刪除使用者](#deleting-a-user)一節。請務必注意，一旦開始永久刪除使用者帳戶即無法復原。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p426">To delete system-generated logs retrieved through an access request, you must remove the user from the service and permanently delete their Azure Active Directory account. For instructions about permanently delete a user, see the [Deleting a user section](#deleting-a-user) in this guide. It's important to note that permanently deleting a user account is irreversible once initiated.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1600">永久刪除使用者帳戶會將 30 天內近乎所有 Office 365 服務上的使用者資料，從系統產生的記錄中移除，可能危及服務安全性或穩定性的資料除外。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1600">Permanently deleting a user account removes the user's data from system-generated logs, except for data that may compromise the security or stability of the service, for nearly all Office 365 services within 30 days.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1601">此 30 天期限的一個例外是，在 Exchange Online 中永久刪除使用者帳戶所需的時間超過 30 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1601">One exception to this 30-day period is that the permanent deletion of the user account in Exchange Online takes longer than 30 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1602">這是因為 Exchange Online 內容的重要本質，並且為了防止資料意外外洩。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1602">This is due to the critical nature of Exchange Online content and to prevent accidental data loss.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1603">Exchange Online已經過設計，在永久刪除了使用者帳戶之後，會故意將資料置於保留狀態最多 60 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1603">Exchange Online has been engineered to intentionally place data in a holding state for up to 60 days after a user account has been permanently deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1604">若要在 30 天時間範圍內永久刪除使用者的 Exchange Online 資料，請永久刪除 Azure Active Directory 中的使用者帳戶，然後連絡 [Microsoft 支援](https://support.microsoft.com/)，並要求在排定的刪除程序外手動移除使用者的 Exchange Online 資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1604">To permanently delete a user's Exchange Online data in a 30-day time frame, permanently delete the user account in Azure Active Directory and then contact [Microsoft Support](https://support.microsoft.com/) and request that the user's Exchange Online data be manually removed outside the scheduled delete process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1605">如需詳細資訊，請參閱本指南先前所述的[移除 Exchange Online 資料](#removing-exchange-online-data)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1605">For more information, see [Removing Exchange Online data](#removing-exchange-online-data), which was previously explained in this guide</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p428">刪除使用者帳戶不會移除系統為 Yammer 和 Kaizala 所產生的記錄。若要從這些應用程式中移除資料，請參閱以下其中一項：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p428">Deleting a user's account will not remove system-generated logs for Yammer and Kaizala. To remove the data from these applications, see one of the following:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1608">Yammer - [管理 Yammer Enterprise 中的 GDPR 資料主體要求](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1608">Yammer - [Manage GDPR data subject requests in Yammer Enterprise](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1609">Kaizala - [在 Kaizala 中匯出或刪除使用者的組織資料](/office365/kaizala/export-or-delete-a-user-s-data)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1609">Kaizala - [Export or delete a user's organizational data in Kaizala](/office365/kaizala/export-or-delete-a-user-s-data)</span></span>

#### <a name="national-clouds"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1610">國家雲</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1610">National clouds</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1611">全域 IT 系統管理員必須執行下列動作來匯出下列國家雲中系統所產生的記錄資料：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1611">A global IT admin needs to do the following to export system-generated log data in the following national clouds:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1612">**Office 365 Germany**：請依照上述步驟進行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1612">**Office 365 Germany**: Follow the steps above.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1613">**Office 365 US Government**：[移至 Office 365 系統管理入口網站](https://portal.office365.us)，將要求提交給 Microsoft 支援服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1613">**Office 365 US Government**: [Go to the Office 365 admin portal](https://portal.office365.us) and submit a request to Microsoft Support.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1614">**由 21Vianet (中國) 營運的 Office 365**：[移至由 21Vianet 營運的 Office 365 系統管理入口網站](https://portal.partner.microsoftonline.cn/AdminPortal/Home#/homepage)、移至 [商務]   >  [訂用帳戶]  >  [隱私權]  >  [GDPR]，然後輸入必要的資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1614">**Office 365 operated by 21Vianet (China)**: [Go to the Office 365 operated by 21Vianet admin portal](https://portal.partner.microsoftonline.cn/AdminPortal/Home#/homepage) and then go to **Commerce** > **Subscription** > **Privacy** > **GDPR** and enter the required information.</span></span>

## <a name="part-4-additional-resources-to-assist-you-with-dsrs"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1615">第 4 部分：其他協助您使用 DSR 的資源</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1615">Part 4: Additional resources to assist you with DSRs</span></span>

### <a name="dsr-guides-for-other-microsoft-enterprise-services"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1616">Microsoft 企業服務的 DSR 指引</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1616">DSR guides for other Microsoft enterprise services</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p429">本指南的主題專注於使用 Office 365 產品、服務及系統管理工具時，如何尋找並處理個人資料以回應 DSR。請移至 [Microsoft 服務信任入口網站](https://servicetrust.microsoft.com/)，來存取其他 Microsoft 企業服務的類似指引。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p429">This guide is dedicated to the topic of how to find and act on personal data to respond to DSRs when using Office 365 products, services, and administrative tools. Go to the [Microsoft Service Trust Portal](https://servicetrust.microsoft.com/) to access similar guides for other Microsoft enterprise services.</span></span>

### <a name="microsoft-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1619">Microsoft 支援</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1619">Microsoft Support</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p430">「支援資料」是您和您的使用者在貴組織或您的使用者與 Microsoft 接洽，以接收與 Office 365 或其他 Microsoft 產品和服務相關的產品支援 (例如對非預期的產品行為進行疑難排解) 時，提供給 Microsoft 的資料。如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [GDPR 的 Microsoft 支援與專業服務資料主體要求](/microsoft-365/compliance/gdpr-dsr-prof-services)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p430">"Support Data" is the data you and your users provide to Microsoft if your organization or your users engage with Microsoft to receive product support related to Office 365 or other Microsoft products and services (for example, to troubleshoot unexpected product behavior). Some of this data may contain personal data. For more information, see [Microsoft Support and Professional Services Data Subject Requests for the GDPR](/microsoft-365/compliance/gdpr-dsr-prof-services).</span></span>

### <a name="product-and-services-authenticated-with-an-org-id-for-which-microsoft-is-a-data-controller"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1623">使用組織識別碼驗證的產品和服務，Microsoft 是其資料控制者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1623">Product and services authenticated with an Org ID for which Microsoft is a data controller</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p431">本指南的第 1 至 3 部分涵蓋 Microsoft 是貴組織之資料處理者的產品和服務，因此 DSR 功能可供您的租用戶系統管理員使用。有各種不同情況，其中貴組織的使用者可能使用其公司或學校帳戶 (也稱為「Azure Active Directory 識別碼」或「AAD」) 來登入 Microsoft 是資料控制者的 Microsoft 產品和服務。對於所有這類產品和服務，您的使用者必須直接向 Microsoft 提出資料主體要求，而且 Microsoft 將會直接對使用者履行要求。經由設計，涉及儲存使用者撰寫內容的產品和服務可讓使用者存取、匯出、修正和刪除其使用者撰寫的內容，這是產品既有產品功能的一部分。可能適用此情況的情節如下：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p431">Parts 1–3 of this guide covers products and services for which Microsoft is a data processor to your organization, and thus DSR capability is made available to your tenant administrator. There are various circumstances where your organization's users may use their work or school account (also referred to as "Azure Active Directory ID" or "AAD") to sign in to Microsoft products and services for which Microsoft is a data controller. For all such products and services, your users need to initiate their own data subject requests directly to Microsoft and Microsoft will fulfill the requests directly to the user. By design, products and services involving storage of user-authored content enable users to access, export, rectify, and delete their user-authored content as part of the inherent functionality of the products. Scenarios where this may apply include the following:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1629">**選擇性連線的線上服務：** 企業用 Microsoft 365 應用程式會使特定選擇性連線的線上服務可供使用者使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1629">**Optional connected online services:** Microsoft 365 Apps for enterprise makes certain optional connected online services available to the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1630">服務和相關使用者控制項的清單會列在[這裡](https://support.office.com/article/microsoft-s-other-connected-services-92c234f1-dc91-4dc1-925d-6c90fc3816d8)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1630">The list of services and related user controls are listed [here](https://support.office.com/article/microsoft-s-other-connected-services-92c234f1-dc91-4dc1-925d-6c90fc3816d8).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1631">您可以決定是否要允許使用者使用這些服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1631">You can decide whether you would like to allow your end users to use these services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1632">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[系統管理員如何在企業用 Microsoft 365 應用程式中管理控制器服務](/DeployOffice/manage-controller-services-office-365-proplus)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1632">For more information, see [How admins can manage controller services in Microsoft 365 Apps for enterprise](/DeployOffice/manage-controller-services-office-365-proplus).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1633">如果這些選擇性服務處理個人資料，Microsoft 是這些服務的資料控制者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1633">If these optional services process personal data, Microsoft is a data controller for these services.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1634">**使用者意見反應：** 如果使用者選擇提供對 Microsoft 產品和服務提供意見反應，則 Microsoft 是這類意見反應的資料控制者，甚至其中包含個人資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1634">**User feedback:** If your users elect to provide feedback on Microsoft products and services, Microsoft is a data controller for such feedback to the extent it contains personal data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1635">Microsoft 將會對 Microsoft 所收集的意見反應履行任何資料主體要求 (包括由 Microsoft 子處理者所管理的意見反應)，但若 Microsoft 已指示使用者不要在意見反應收集過程中包含個人資料，則不在此限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1635">Microsoft fulfills any data subject requests for feedback collected by Microsoft (including feedback managed by Microsoft subprocessors) except in cases where Microsoft has instructed users not to include personal data during the feedback collection process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1636">例外：如果 Microsoft 已指示使用者不要在意見反應收集過程中包含個人資料，則 Microsoft 將信賴該指示，並將假設未提供任何個人資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1636">Exceptions: If Microsoft has instructed users not to include personal data during the feedback collection process, Microsoft relies on that instruction and will assume that no personal data has been provided.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1637">已利用第三方意見反應服務提供者建立個別帳戶的使用者必須直接向那些提供者履行其 DSR。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1637">Users who have created a separate account with third-party feedback service providers need to fulfill their DSR directly with those providers.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1638">**Windows 透過公司或學校帳戶來驗證** - 如果貴組織已購買 Windows 授權，而且您的使用者使用其公司或學校帳戶向組織提供的 Windows 進行驗證，Microsoft 會充當資料控制者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1638">**Windows authenticated via work or school account:** If your organization has purchased Windows licenses, and your users authenticate to organization-provided Windows with their work or school account, Microsoft acts as a data controller.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1639">**使用者取得的產品或服務** - 如果您允許您的使用者以其個人身分取得使用 AAD 進行驗證的 Microsoft 產品或服務 (例如 Office 附加元件或可在 Microsoft Store 取得的應用程式)，Microsoft 可能是資料控制者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1639">**User-acquired products or services:** If you allow your users, acting in their individual capacity, to acquire Microsoft products or services that use AAD for authentication (for example, Office add-ons or applications available in a Microsoft Store), Microsoft may be a data controller.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1640">對於任何這類 Microsoft 產品或服務，使用者必須直接連絡 Microsoft 來發出 DSR。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1640">For any such Microsoft products or services, users need to contact Microsoft directly to initiate a DSR.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p435">如果您刪除透過 Azure Active Directory 啟用的使用者，則您的 (先前) 使用者將無法登入任何產品或服務，其先前倚靠公司或學校帳戶來使用它們。此外，Microsoft 將再也無法驗證與產品或服務之 DSR 要求有關的使用者，Microsoft 是資料控制者。如果您想要讓使用者可以對這類服務發出 DSR，請務必指示您的使用者在刪除使用者的 AAD 帳戶之前先這樣做。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p435">If you delete a user as enabled via Azure Active Directory, your (former) user will lose the ability to sign in to any products or services for which he or she formerly relied upon for a work or school account. Additionally, Microsoft will no longer be able to authenticate the user in connection with a DSR request for products or services for which Microsoft is a data controller. If you wish to enable a user to initiate DSRs against such services, it is important you instruct your user to do so before you delete the user's AAD account.</span></span>

### <a name="personal-accounts"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1644">個人帳戶</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1644">Personal accounts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1645">如果您的使用者已使用 Microsoft 帳戶 (亦即個人帳戶)，從 Microsoft 取得供他們自己使用的產品和服務，而且 Microsoft 是資料控制者，則他們可能會使用 [Microsoft 隱私權儀表板](https://account.microsoft.com/account/privacy)來發出 DSR 要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1645">If your users have used Microsoft accounts (that is, personal accounts) to acquire products and services from Microsoft for their own use and for which Microsoft is a data controller, they may initiate DSR requests by using the [Microsoft privacy dashboard](https://account.microsoft.com/account/privacy).</span></span>

### <a name="third-party-products"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1646">協力廠商產品</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1646">Third-party products</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1647">如果貴組織或您的使用者以其個人身分從協力廠商取得產品和服務，並使用 Microsoft 公司或學校帳戶進行驗證，則任何資料主體要求都應該導向至適當的協力廠商。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1647">If your organization, or your users acting in their individual capacity, have acquired products or services from third parties and use their Microsoft work or school account for authentication, any data subject requests should be directed to the applicable third party.</span></span>

## <a name="appendix-a-preparing-for-dsr-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1648">附錄 A：準備 DSR 調查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1648">Appendix A: Preparing for DSR investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1649">若要準備讓貴組織使用 Office 365 服務進行 DSR 調查，請考慮下列建議：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1649">To help prepare your organization to undertake DSR investigations using Office 365 services, consider the following recommendations:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1650">使用安全性與合規性中心的 DSR 電子文件探索案例工具來管理 DSR 調查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1650">Use the DSR eDiscovery case tool in the Security & Compliance Center to manage DSR investigations</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1651">設定合規性界限來限制內容搜尋的範圍</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1651">Set up Compliance Boundaries to limit the scope of Content Searches</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1652">在 DSR 調查時使用稽核記錄搜尋工具</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1652">Use the audit log search tool in DSR investigations</span></span>

### <a name="use-the-dsr-case-tool-to-manage-dsr-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1653">使用 DSR 案例工具來管理 DSR 調查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1653">Use the DSR case tool to manage DSR investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p436">建議您使用 安全性與合規性中心的 DSR 案例工具，來管理 DSR 調查。使用 DSR 案例工具，您可以：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p436">We recommend that you use the DSR case tool in Security & Compliance Center to manage DSR investigations. By using the DSR case tool, you can:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1656">針對每一個 DSR 調查建立個別案例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1656">Create a separate case for each DSR investigation.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1657">使用內建功能來搜尋與特定資料主體相關的所有內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1657">Use the built-in to search for all content related to a specific data subject.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1658">當建立新的案例並開始搜尋時，會搜尋這些內容位置：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1658">When you create a case and start the search, these content locations are searched:</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1659">您組織中的所有信箱 (包括與所有 Microsoft Teams 和 Microsoft 365 群組相關聯的信箱)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1659">All mailboxes in your organization (including the mailboxes associated with all Microsoft Teams and Microsoft 365 Groups)</span></span>
   - <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1660">貴組織中所有的 Sharepoint 網站和商務用 OneDrive 帳戶</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1660">All SharePoint Online sites and OneDrive for Business accounts in your organization</span></span>
   - <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1661">貴組織中所有的 Microsoft Teams 網站和 Microsoft 365 群組網站</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1661">All Microsoft Teams sites and Microsoft 365 group sites in your organization</span></span>
   - <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1662">Exchange Online 中的所有公用資料夾</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1662">All public folders in Exchange Online</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1663">修改預設搜尋查詢，然後重新執行搜尋來縮小搜尋結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1663">Revise the default search query and rerun the search to narrow the search results.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p438">藉由將人員新增為案例成員，來控制誰有權存取此案例；只有成員才能存取案例，而且在安全性與合規性中心內的 DSR 案例頁面上，他們只能在案例清單上看到自己的案例。此外，您也可以將不同的權限指派給相同案例的不同成員。例如，您可以允許某些成員只能檢視案例和內容搜尋的結果，而允許其他成員建立搜尋並匯出搜尋結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p438">Control who has access to the case by adding people as members of the case; only members can access the case and are only able to see their cases in the list of cases on the DSR cases page in the Security & Compliance Center. Additionally, you can assign different permissions to different members of the same case. For example, you could allow some members to only view the case and the results of a Content Search and allow other members to create searches and export search results.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p439">建立匯出工作來匯出搜尋結果，以回應 DSR 匯出要求。您可以匯出內容搜尋所傳回的所有內容。也會匯出與資料主體相關的其他 Office 365 資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p439">Create export jobs to export the search results in response to a DSR export request. You can export all content returned by the Content Search. Other Office 365 data related to a data subject is also exported.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p440">建立匯出工作來匯出搜尋結果，以回應 DSR 匯出要求。您可以匯出內容搜尋所傳回的所有內容。您可以針對 Office 漫遊服務匯出系統產生的記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p440">Create export jobs to export the search results in response to a DSR export request. You can export all content returned by the Content Search. You can also export system-generated logs for Office Roaming service.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p441">DSR 調查程序完成時，請刪除案例。這會移除與案例相關聯的所有內容搜尋和匯出工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p441">Delete cases when the DSR investigation process is complete. This removes all the content searches and export jobs associated with the case.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1675">若要開始使用 DSR 案例，請參閱[使用安全性與合規性中心的 DSR 案例工具來管理 GDPR 資料主體要求](/microsoft-365/compliance/manage-gdpr-data-subject-requests-with-the-dsr-case-tool)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1675">To get started with using DSR cases, see [Manage GDPR data subject requests with the DSR case tool in the Security & Compliance Center](/microsoft-365/compliance/manage-gdpr-data-subject-requests-with-the-dsr-case-tool).</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p442">電子文件探索管理員可以檢視和管理貴組織中所有的 DSR 案例。如需有關不同電子文件探索角色的詳細資訊，請參閱[將電子文件探索權限指派給潛在案例成員](/Office365/SecurityCompliance/assign-ediscovery-permissions) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p442">An eDiscovery Administrator can view and manage all DSR cases in your organization. For more information about the different roles related to eDiscovery, see [Assign eDiscovery permissions to potential case members](/Office365/SecurityCompliance/assign-ediscovery-permissions).</span></span>

### <a name="set-up-compliance-boundaries-to-limit-the-scope-of-content-searches"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1678">設定合規性界限來限制內容搜尋的範圍</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1678">Set up Compliance Boundaries to limit the scope of Content Searches</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p443">您可以使用安全性與合規性中心的搜尋權限篩選功能，來實作合規性界限。合規性界限會在組織內建立邏輯搜尋界限，以控制/限制 IT 系統管理員或法務人員可以搜尋哪些內容位置 (例如 Exchange Online 信箱和 SharePoint Online 網站)。對於需要遵守地理界限的跨國組織、需要區隔不同機構的政府組織，以及隔離成業務單位或部門的企業組織，合規性界限會很有用。對於上述所有情況，合規性界限都可以用於 DSR 調查，以限制參與調查的人員可以搜尋的信箱和網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p443">Compliance Boundaries are implemented by using the search permissions filtering functionality in the Security & Compliance Center. Compliance Boundaries create logical search boundaries within an organization that control/limit which content locations (for example Exchange Online mailboxes and SharePoint Online sites) that an IT admin or compliance officer can search. Compliance Boundaries are useful for multi-national organizations that need to respect geographical boundaries, governmental organizations that need to separate different agencies, and business organizations that segregated into business unit or department. For all these scenarios, Compliance Boundaries can be used in DSR investigations to limit which mailboxes and sites can be searched by people involved in the investigation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1683">您可以搭配使用合規性界限與電子文件探索案例，將可在調查中搜尋的內容位置僅限制為機構或業務單位內的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1683">You can use Compliance Boundaries together with eDiscovery cases to limit the content locations that can be searched in an investigation to those locations only within the agency or business unit.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1684">以下是如何針對 DSR 調查實作合規性界限 (與電子文件探索案例搭配) 的高階概觀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1684">Here's a high-level overview of how to implement Compliance Boundaries (together with eDiscovery cases) for DSR investigations.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1685">決定貴組織中要指定為合規性界限的機構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1685">Determine the agencies in your organization that will be designated as a compliance boundary.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p444">決定 Azure Active Directory 中哪個使用者物件屬性將用來定義合規性界限。例如，您也可以選擇 Country、CountryCode 或 Department 屬性，以便您在下一個步驟中建立的系統管理員角色群組的成員只能搜尋對該屬性具有特定值之使用者的內容位置。這是您限制誰可以搜尋特定機構中內容的方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p444">Determine which user object attribute in Azure Active Directory will be used to define the compliance boundary. For example, you might choose the Country, CountryCode, or Department attribute, so that members of the admin role group that you create in the next step can only search the content locations of the users that have a specific value for that attribute. This is how you limit who can search for content in a specific agency.</span></span>

   > [!NOTE]
   > <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1689">目前，您必須對商務用 OneDrive 執行額外步驟，並將 Microsoft 支援服務歸檔，讓屬性同步至商務用 OneDrive 帳戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1689">Currently, you must perform an additional step for OneDrive for Business and file a Microsoft Support request to have the attribute synchronized to OneDrive for Business accounts.</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p445">在安全性與合規性中心，對每一個合規性界限建立系統管理員角色群組。我們建議您複製內建的電子文件探索管理員角色群組，然後視需要移除任何角色，來建立這些角色群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p445">Create an admin role group in the Security & Compliance Center for each compliance boundary. We recommend that you create these role groups by copying the built-in eDiscovery Manager role group and then removing any roles as necessary.</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p446">請將成員新增至每個特定角色群組，作為電子文件探索管理員。成員將是負責調查並回應 DSR 的人員，而且通常包括 IT 系統管理員、資料隱私權主管、合規性管理員，以及人力資源代表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p446">Add members to each of the specific role groups as eDiscovery Mangers. Members are the people responsible for investigating and responding to DSRs, and will typically consist of IT admins, data privacy officers, compliance managers, and human resource representatives.</span></span>

5. <span data-ttu-id="997d0-p447">請建立每個合規性界限的搜尋權限篩選器，如此對應的系統管理員角色群組成員，就只能搜尋該機構/合規性界限規內使用者的信箱和網站。搜尋權限篩選器讓對應的角色群組成員，只能搜尋使用者物件屬性值對應至機構/合規性界限規的內容位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p447">Create a search permissions filter for each compliance boundary so that the members of the corresponding admin role group can only search mailboxes and sites for users within that agency/compliance boundary. The search permissions filter allows members of the corresponding role group to search only the content locations with user object attribute value that corresponds to the agency/compliance boundary.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1696">如需逐步指示，請參閱[設定 Office 365 中電子文件探索調查的合規性界限](/microsoft-365/compliance/set-up-compliance-boundaries)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1696">For step-by-step instructions, see [Set up compliance boundaries for eDiscovery investigations in Office 365](/microsoft-365/compliance/set-up-compliance-boundaries).</span></span>

### <a name="use-the-audit-log-search-tool-in-dsr-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1697">在 DSR 調查時使用稽核記錄搜尋工具</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1697">Use the audit log search tool in DSR investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-p448">IT 系統管理員可以使用安全性與合規性中心的稽核記錄搜尋工具，來識別使用者已建立、存取、變更或刪除的文件、檔案和其他 Office 365 資源。搜尋此類型的活動有助於 DSR 調查。例如，在 SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 中，使用者執行下列活動時，會記錄稽核事件：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-p448">IT admins can use the audit log search tool in the Security & Compliance Center to identity documents, files, and other Office 365 resources that users have created, accessed, changed, or deleted. Searching for this kind activity can be useful in DSR investigations. For example, in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business, auditing events are logged when users perform these activities:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1701">已存取檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1701">Accessed a file</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1702">已修改檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1702">Modified a file</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1703">已移動檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1703">Moved a file</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1704">已上傳或下載檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1704">Uploaded or downloaded a file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1705">您可以搜尋特定活動的稽核記錄、活動類型、特定使用者所執行的活動，以及其他搜尋準則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1705">You can search the audit log for specific activities, types of activities, activities performed by a specific user, and other search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1706">除了 SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 活動外，您也可以搜尋 Flow、Power BI 和 Microsoft Teams 中的活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1706">In addition to SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business activities, you can also search for activities in Flow, Power BI, and Microsoft Teams.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1707">稽核記錄會保留 90 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1707">Auditing records are retained for 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1708">因此，您將無法搜尋 90 天以前發生的使用者活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1708">Therefore, you won't be able to search for user activities that occurred more than 90 days ago.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1709">如需稽核活動的完整清單，以及如何搜尋稽核記錄，請參閱[搜尋安全性與合規性中心的稽核記錄](/microsoft-365/compliance/search-the-audit-log-in-security-and-compliance)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1709">For a complete list of audited activities and how to search the audit log, see [Search the audit log in the Security & Compliance Center](/microsoft-365/compliance/search-the-audit-log-in-security-and-compliance).</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="997d0-1710">若要解決上述的 90 天限制，並維護貴組織稽核記錄的執行歷程記錄，您可以根據週期性排程 (例如，每隔 30 天) 匯出所有活動，以具有貴組織稽核記錄的連續記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1710">To work around the 90-day limitation discussed above and maintain a running history of your organization's auditing records, you could export all activities on a recurring schedule (for example, every 30 days) to have a continuous record of your organization's auditing records.</span></span>

## <a name="appendix-b-change-log"></a><span data-ttu-id="997d0-1711">附錄 B：變更記錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1711">Appendix B: Change log</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="997d0-1712">下表列出自從 2018 年 5 月 25 日首次發行之後，Office 365 DSR 指南中所做的變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="997d0-1712">The following table lists the changes to the Office 365 DSR guide since its initial publication on May 25, 2018.</span></span>
